\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix tile gaps in Chromium-\/based browsers (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8891}{\texttt{\#8891}} by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}})
\item Fix vector drifts when {\ttfamily zoom\+Animation} is {\ttfamily false} and zooming via {\ttfamily fly\+To} or pinch (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8794}{\texttt{\#8794}} by \href{https://github.com/plainheart}{\texttt{@plainheart}})
\item Ensure {\ttfamily to\+Geo\+JSON()} still works with an empty array (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8737}{\texttt{\#8737}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Ensure {\ttfamily Line\+Util} and {\ttfamily Poly\+Util} only iterate over array values and not properties (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8840}{\texttt{\#8840}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Fix rounding errors in center calculation of {\ttfamily Line\+Util} and {\ttfamily Poly\+Util} for small layers (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8784}{\texttt{\#8784}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Prevent unwanted layer toggle while expanding the Layers control on mobile (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8910}{\texttt{\#8910}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Fix an error when a focusing on a {\ttfamily Tooltip}-\/bound {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} that contains a layer without a {\ttfamily get\+Element} method (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8890}{\texttt{\#8890}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Fix {\ttfamily Tooltip} is not showing when loaded dynamically while moving the map (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8672}{\texttt{\#8672}} by \href{https://github.com/theGOTOguy}{\texttt{@the\+GOTOguy}})
\item Fix {\ttfamily no\+Move\+Start} option not applying to {\ttfamily fit\+Bounds} (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8911}{\texttt{\#8911}} by \href{https://github.com/AbdullahSohail-SE}{\texttt{@Abdullah\+Sohail-\/\+SE}})
\item Fix outlines showing up when interacting with the map on Safari 16.\+4+ (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8917}{\texttt{\#8917}} by \href{https://github.com/jonkoops}{\texttt{@jonkoops}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1507}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+9.\+3 (2022-\/11-\/18)}{1.\+9.\+3 (2022-\/11-\/18)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1507}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ⚠️ Drop ESM entrypoint from package because of numerous compatibility issues with plugins (import {\ttfamily leaflet/\+dist/\+leaflet-\/src.\+esm.\+js} explicitly instead to take advantage; ESM by default will come in v2) (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8493}{\texttt{\#8493}} by \href{https://github.com/jonkoops}{\texttt{@jonkoops}})
\item Fix a bug where tooltips could throw an error with canvas renderer (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8498}{\texttt{\#8498}} by \href{https://github.com/Falke-Design}{\texttt{@Falke-\/\+Design}})
\item Fix a bug with incorrect marker popup location when there are multiple markers registered to the same popup (\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/8523}{\texttt{\#8523}} by \href{https://github.com/raychanks}{\texttt{@raychanks}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1512}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{🧪 Tests}{🧪 Tests}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1512}

\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1592}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug fixes}{Bug fixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1592}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Avoid extra {\ttfamily L.\+Canvas} redraws on several scenarios (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5034}{\texttt{\#5250}}, also thanks to \href{https://github.com/manubb}{\texttt{@manubb}} for investigation and PR).
\item Fix behaviour of {\ttfamily dblclick} events in \href{https://developers.google.com/web/updates/2016/11/nic55\#pointer-events}{\texttt{Chrome 55 due to {\ttfamily Pointer\+Event}s}} (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5185}{\texttt{\#5185}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5248}{\texttt{\#5248}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5268}{\texttt{\#5268}}).
\item Fix a dangling comma making IE8 fail to parse the code (by \href{https://github.com/batje}{\texttt{@batje}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5270}{\texttt{\#5270}}).
\item Backport event handling fixes from \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5054}{\texttt{\#5054}} into {\ttfamily L.\+SVG.\+VML} for IE8 (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5215}{\texttt{\#5215}}).
\item Fix a race condition when closing popups during their {\ttfamily popupopen} event (by \href{https://github.com/hagai26}{\texttt{@hagai26}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5202}{\texttt{\#5202}}).
\item Fix {\ttfamily get\+Bounds\+Zoom} return value on CRSs with a flipped axis (by \href{https://github.com/computerlove}{\texttt{@computerlove}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5204}{\texttt{\#5204}}).
\item Avoid infinite loops when the {\ttfamily error\+Tile\+Url} of a {\ttfamily L.\+Tile\+Layer} returns 404 (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5177}{\texttt{\#5177}}).
\item Remove erroneous initialization of unused event listeners (by \href{https://github.com/Brikky}{\texttt{@Brikky}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5160}{\texttt{\#5160}}).
\item Fix rounding of {\ttfamily L.\+Canvas} redraw areas to avoid artifacts during partial updates (by \href{https://github.com/Ernie23}{\texttt{@Ernie23}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5148}{\texttt{\#5148}}).
\item Fix {\ttfamily is\+Popup\+Open()} behaviour of {\ttfamily L.\+Layer} when no popup is bound to a layer (by \href{https://github.com/gvangool}{\texttt{@gvangool}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5106}{\texttt{\#5106}}).
\item Add a sanity check in {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds.\+contains()} to allow for non-\/instantiated {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} objects (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5135}{\texttt{\#5135}}).
\item Fix collapsing of {\ttfamily L.\+Control.\+Layers} when the {\ttfamily collapse} option is {\ttfamily false} (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5131}{\texttt{\#5131}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1593}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{API changes}{API changes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1593}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new {\ttfamily Wrap\+Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} method to {\ttfamily L.\+CRS}, to fix an issue with {\ttfamily max\+Bounds} of {\ttfamily Grid\+Layer}s (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5185}{\texttt{\#5185}}, also thanks to \href{https://github.com/DiogoMCampos}{\texttt{@Diogo\+MCampos}} for investigation).
\item {\ttfamily L.\+Map.\+get\+Size()} will now return {\ttfamily 0} instead of {\ttfamily NaN} in non-\/graphical environments (by \href{https://github.com/ughitsaaron}{\texttt{@ughitsaaron}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5209}{\texttt{\#5209}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1594}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Improvements}{Improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1594}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Several minor documentation improvements by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/jieter}{\texttt{@jieter}}, \href{https://github.com/alonsogarciapablo}{\texttt{@alonsogarciapablo}}, \href{https://github.com/jasonoverland}{\texttt{@jasonoverland}}, \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}, \href{https://github.com/ghybs}{\texttt{@ghybs}}, \href{https://github.com/Ralf8686}{\texttt{@Ralf8686}}, \href{https://github.com/geoloep}{\texttt{@geoloep}}
\item Add an {\ttfamily alt} attribute to the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}img\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}s of marker shadows (by \href{https://github.com/topicus}{\texttt{@topicus}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5259}{\texttt{\#5259}}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1595}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+0.\+2 (2016-\/11-\/21)}{1.\+0.\+2 (2016-\/11-\/21)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1595}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1596}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug fixes}{Bug fixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1596}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fix CSS for marker shadows when {\ttfamily max-\/width} is already set (by \href{https://github.com/brunob}{\texttt{@brunob}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5046}{\texttt{\#5046}}).
\item Fix canvas redraw when style updates fill and/\+or weight (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5034}{\texttt{\#5034}}).
\item Prevent canvas from firing multiple {\ttfamily mouseover} events for same layer (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5033}{\texttt{\#5033}}).
\item Fixed a race condition when removing and adding {\ttfamily L.\+Canvas} vectors during a zoom animation (by \href{https://github.com/ghybs}{\texttt{@ghybs}}) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5011}{\texttt{\#5011}}.
\item Fix zoom animation of Image\+Overlay when CRS\textquotesingle{}s Y axis is flipped (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/4993}{\texttt{\#4993}}.
\item Fix encoding/\+decoding of Geo\+JSON {\ttfamily Feature\+Collection}s (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/5045}{\texttt{\#5045}}.
\item Fix {\ttfamily min\+Zoom}/\+{\ttfamily max\+Zoom} late inizialization (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/4916}{\texttt{\#4916}}.
\item Fix styling of custom SVG markers by making stricter CSS selectors (by \href{https://github.com/jwoyame}{\texttt{@jwoyame}}) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/4597}{\texttt{\#4597}}.
\item Fix order of {\ttfamily mouseover}/\+{\ttfamily mouseout} events on overlapping {\ttfamily L.\+Canvas} layers (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5090}{\texttt{\#5090}}.
\item Fix drag behaviour when a draggable marker is removed in mid-\/drag (by \href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{@Ivan\+Sanchez}}, \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5063}{\texttt{\#5063}}.
\item Fix {\ttfamily L.\+Control.\+Layers.\+collapse()} on initially uncollapsed layer controls (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5131}{\texttt{\#5131}}.
\item Fix blurriness of {\ttfamily L.\+Tooltip} by rounding up pixel coordinates (by \href{https://github.com/ashmigelski}{\texttt{@ashmigelski}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5089}{\texttt{\#5089}}.
\item Fix click events on overlapping geometries when using {\ttfamily L.\+Canvas} (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}), \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/5100}{\texttt{\#5100}}.

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item Event listeners are now always called in the order they have been registered, while until rc2 listeners with a context were all called before listeners without context (even if registered later), and the listeners with context were called in an unpredictable order (by \href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{@yohanboniface}}) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/4769}{\texttt{\#4769}}

Beta 2 fixes over 50 bugs that were reported by users trying out beta 1. The vast majority of changes are small fixes to problems that are triggered in very specific situations or conditions, a few API consolidation changes, and a few browser workarounds.\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1619}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{API changes}{API changes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1619}

\item Fixed an edge case of \`{}L.Circle.\+get\+Bounds()\`{} (by \+[@knabar]\+(\href{https://github.com/knabar}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+knabar}})) \+[\#3776]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3776}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3776}})
\item Fixed \`{}\+Rectangle.set\+Bounds()\`{} return value (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/commit/e698f641afadd4a0b412a6c9e065a6dbfbe16f44}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+commit/\+e698f641afadd4a0b412a6c9e065a6dbfbe16f44}}
\item Fixed event firing order when opening a popup (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3745]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3745}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3745}})
\item Fixed tile layer loading when dragging then immediately pinch-\/zooming the map (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \+[\#3814]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3814}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3814}})
\item Work around browser limitations when panning the map too far away (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}}) and \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \+[\#3608]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3608}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3608}})
\item Fixed popup text selection and touch events for IE 10 (by \+[@danzel]\+(\href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+danzel}})) \+[\#3804]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3804}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3804}})
\item Fixed tile layer ordering when \`{}max\+Zoom\`{} is set (by \+[@patrickarlt]\+(\href{https://github.com/patrickarlt}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+patrickarlt}})) \+[\#3721]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3721}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3721}})
\item Fixed scale behaviour on non-\/standard CRSs (by \+[@javimolla]\+(\href{https://github.com/patrickarlt}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+patrickarlt}}), special thanks to \+[Your First PR]\+(\href{https://yourfirstpr.github.io/}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+yourfirstpr.\+github.\+io/\+}})) \+[\#2990]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2990}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2990}})
\item Fixed rendering of off-\/screen vector layers (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3836]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3836}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3836}})
\item Fixed rendering of intersecting vector layers (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3583]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3583}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3583}})
\item Enforced stricter code linting
\item Fixed disabled drag handlers not being able to be re-\/enabled (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3825]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3825}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3825}})
\item Fixed panning outside the map bounds (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3878]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3878}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3878}})
\item Worked around IE 11 not focusing the map using keyboard (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \+[\#3772]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3772}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3772}})
\item Fixed vector layer positioning during a zoom animation in low zoom (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \+[\#3769]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3769}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3769}})
\item Implemented \`{}no\+Wrap\`{} option in \`{}L.Grid\+Layer\`{} (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})) \+[\#3691]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3691}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3691}})
\item Fixed popups panning the map while running another pan animation (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3744]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3744}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3744}})
\item Fixed uncorrect length of scale control due to CSS styles (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3668]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3668}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3668}})
\item Fixed detection of default image path for icons (by \+[@ilfa]\+(\href{https://github.com/ilfa}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+ilfa}})) \+[\#3770]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3770}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3770}})
\item Various Canvas events fixes (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3917]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3917}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3917}})
\item Fix touch scroll in layers control (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#2882]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2882}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2882}})
\item Fix duration not passed through from set\+View to pan\+By (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})) \+[\#3300]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3300}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3300}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1622}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+0-\/beta1 (2015-\/07-\/14)}{1.\+0-\/beta1 (2015-\/07-\/14)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1622}
The first beta of the huge, long-\/awaited Leaflet 1.\+0 release.

This version contains a lot of beneficial but potentially breaking changes (especially if you\textquotesingle{}re a plugin author), so please read through the changes carefully if your code breaks after upgrading.\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1623}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Vectors API improvements}{Vectors API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1623}
Leaflet vector layers rendering got a major rewrite, making it possible to switch between rendering backends (Canvas, SVG) dynamically (and even use both for different layers at the same time), have more than one physical pane for vector layers, significantly improving performance, adding Canvas retina support, getting rid of ugly hacks and generally making the code much cleaner. Main PR \+[\#2290]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2290}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2290}}).


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added \`{}\+Renderer\`{} layer (inherited by SVG/\+\+Canvas implementations) that handles renderer bounds and zoom animation.
\item Added \`{}\+SVG\`{} \& \`{}\+Canvas\`{} classes that now contain all renderer-\/specific code for vector layers and can be added as layers to the map.
\item All vector layer classes (\`{}\+Path\`{}, \`{}\+Polyline\`{}, etc.) now don\textquotesingle{}t contain any renderer-\/specific code and instead can be passed a renderer layer to use as \`{}renderer\`{} in options;
\item Removed \`{}\+Multi\+Polyline\`{} and \`{}\+Multi\+Polygon\`{} classes since multiple rings are now handled by \`{}\+Polyline\`{} and \`{}\+Polygon\`{} classes respectively. Layers with multiple rings now perform much better (since each is now physically a single path object instead of being a \`{}\+Feature\+Group\`{} of layers).
\item \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+Dramatically improved performance of interactive Canvas layers\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. Mouse events work much faster (due to improved hit detection algorithms), and layers get updated many times faster (with partial redraws instead of redrawing the whole Canvas).
\item \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+Dramatically improved performance of interactive SVG layers\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} (e.\+g. creating a big Geo\+JSON layer and adding to a map got 3x faster while taking 2.\+5x less memory). \+[\#2240]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2240}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2240}}) \+[\#2315]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2315}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2315}})
\item Added retina support for Canvas layers.
\item Improved default vector layer styles.
\item Added \`{}\+Polyline\`{} and \`{}\+Polygon\`{} \`{}get\+Center\`{} for getting centroids.
\item Respectively, improved \`{}\+Polyline\`{} and \`{}\+Polygon\`{} popup positioning when calling \`{}open\+Popup\`{}.
\item Improved \`{}\+Polyline\`{}/\+\`{}\+Polygon\`{} \`{}get\+Bounds\`{} to be cached (so it works much faster).
\item Changed \`{}\+Circle\`{} to inherit from \`{}\+Circle\+Marker\`{} and not the other way.
\item Fixed \`{}\+Geo\+JSON\`{} \`{}reset\+Style\`{} to work properly in case \`{}style\`{} option wasn\textquotesingle{}t set.
\item Fixed a bug where map fired \`{}moveend\`{} when updating Canvas layers.
\item Removed \`{}\+Polyline\`{} and \`{}\+Polygon\`{} \`{}splice\+Lat\+Lngs\`{} method (just use \`{}set\+Lat\+Lngs\`{} instead).
\item Changed \`{}\+Polygon\`{} \`{}get\+Lat\+Lngs\`{} to always return an array of rings (nested array) (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#2618]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2618}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2618}}) \+[\#3386]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3386}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3386}}) \+[Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet\#3279]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3279}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3279}}) \+[\#2648]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2648}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2648}})
\item Added the ability to specify a custom pane for vector layers (making it possible to easily do stacks like vectors-\/tiles-\/vectors with proper z-\/index order) (by \+[@\+Jakobud]\+(\href{https://github.com/Jakobud}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Jakobud}})). \+[\#3266]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3266}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3266}}) \+[\#2786]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2786}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2786}})
\item Added vector layers \`{}fill\+Rule\`{} option (by \+[@bullgare]\+(\href{https://github.com/bullgare}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+bullgare}})). \+[\#2834]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2834}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2834}})
\item Removed \`{}\+L\+\_\+\+PREFER\+\_\+\+CANVAS\`{} global switch and added \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}prefer\+Canvas\`{} option instead (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#3623]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3623}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3623}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1624}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Layers API improvements}{Layers API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1624}
All Leaflet layers (including markers, popups, tile and vector layers) have been refactored to have a common parent, \`{}\+Layer\`{} class, that shares the basic logic of adding and removing. The leads to the following changes (main PR \+[\#2266]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2266}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2266}})):\+


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added \`{}\+Layer\`{} class which all layers added to a map should inherit from.
\item Added \`{}add\`{} and \`{}remove\`{} events to all layers.
\item Added \`{}remove\`{} method to layers and controls (\`{}marker.remove()\`{} is now equivalent to \`{}map.remove\+Layer(marker)\`{}).
\item Improved performance of adding and removing layers.
\item Added \`{}pane\`{} option to all layers that can be changed (e.\+g. you can set \`{}pane:\+ \textquotesingle{}overlay\+Pane\textquotesingle{}\`{} to a tile layer).
\item Added \`{}map\`{} \`{}create\+Pane\`{} method for custom panes. \+[\#1742]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1742}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1742}})
\item Simplified map panes --- removed \`{}objects\+Pane\`{}, all panes are on the same level now.
\item Added \`{}shadow\+Pane\`{} option to markers as well.
\item Added \`{}get\+Events\`{} method to all layers that returns an \`{}\{event:\+ listener, ...\}\`{} hash; layers now manage its listeners automatically without having to do this in \`{}on\+Add\`{}/\+\`{}on\+Remove\`{}.
\item Added \`{}toggle\+Popup\`{}, \`{}set\+Popup\+Content\`{}, \`{}get\+Popup\`{}, \`{}is\+Popup\+Open\`{} methods to all layers. \+[\#2279]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2279}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2279}}) \+[\#2292]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2292}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2292}})
\item Improved performance of adding/\+removing layers with layers control present (instead of listening to any layer add/\+remove, the control only listens to layers added in configuration).
\item Fixed \`{}\+Feature\+Group\`{} \`{}get\+Bounds\`{} to work correctly when containing circle markers.
\item Removed \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}tilelayersload\`{} event.
\item Removed \`{}\+Popup\`{} \`{}open\`{} and \`{}close\`{} events in favor of \`{}add\`{} and \`{}remove\`{} for consistency.
\item Moved all layer-\/related logic in \`{}\+Map.js\`{} to \`{}\+Layer.js\`{}.
\item Improved \`{}\+Feature\+Group\`{} \`{}bind\+Popup\`{} to accept a function for generating popup content, significantly improving memory footprint when adding popups to a huge number of layers (by \+[@patrickarlt]\+(\href{https://github.com/patrickarlt}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+patrickarlt}})). \+[\#3109]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3109}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3109}}) \+[\#3059]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3059}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3059}})
\item Added \`{}\+Image\+Overlay\`{} interactivity (mouse events, etc.) (by \+[@snkashis]\+(\href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+snkashis}})). \+[\#3009]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3009}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3009}}) \+[\#1727]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1727}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1727}})
\item Added \`{}\+Image\+Overlay\`{} \`{}get\+Bounds\`{} (by \+[@brunob]\+(\href{https://github.com/brunob}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+brunob}})). \+[\#2848]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2848}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2848}})
\item Renamed \`{}clickable\`{} option to \`{}interactive\`{} (by \+[@\+Andrii\+Heonia]\+(\href{https://github.com/AndriiHeonia}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Andrii\+Heonia}})). \+[\#2838]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2838}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2838}}) \+[\#2499]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2499}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2499}})
\item Changed the default z-\/index of panes to be bigger, leaving more room for customization (by \+[@patrickarlt]\+(\href{https://github.com/patrickarlt}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+patrickarlt}})). \+[\#3591]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3591}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3591}})
\item Improved DOM event bubbling mechanism for layers (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet\#3307]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3307}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3307}}) \+[\#3450]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3450}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3450}}) \+[\#3307]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3307}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3307}})
\item Added \`{}non\+Bubbling\+Events\`{} option to layers (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#3605]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3605}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3605}}) \+[\#3307]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3307}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3307}}) \+[\#3604]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3604}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3604}})
\end{DoxyItemize}

In addition, layer events implementation was rewritten to use \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}event delegation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, significantly improving add/\+remove performance and memory footprint. \+[\#3032]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3032}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3032}}) \+[\#46]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/46}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+46}})\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1625}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Tile\+Layer \& Projections API improvements}{Tile\+Layer \& Projections API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1625}
Tile\+Layer code and everything projections-\/related has undergone a major refactoring, documented in PR \+[\#2247]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2247}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2247}}). It includes the following changes (in addition to much cleaner and simpler code):\+\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1626}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Tile\+Layer API improvements}{Tile\+Layer API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1626}
These changes make implementing custom grid-\/like layers for Leaflet much easier.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Moved most of the \`{}\+Tile\+Layer\`{} logic into the new \`{}\+Grid\+Layer\`{} class (which \`{}\+Tile\+Layer\`{} now inherits, extending it with logic specific to tile servers).
\item Removed \`{}\+Tile\+Layer.Canvas\`{} in favor of the much more flexible and powerful \`{}\+Grid\+Layer\`{}.
\item Improved tile wrapping and bounding logic in \`{}\+Tile\+Layer\`{} to work transparently and completely depent on the CRS used; removed the need for \`{}\+Tile\+Layer\`{} hacks when using custom projections.
\item Added non-\/square tiles support (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})). \+[\#3573]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3573}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3573}}) \+[\#3570]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3570}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3570}})
\item Removed \`{}url\`{} property in \`{}tileload\`{} and \`{}tileloadstart\`{} events (get it through \`{}tile.src\`{}).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1627}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Projections API improvements}{Projections API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1627}
These changes were targeted at removing any hardcoded projection-\/specific logic accross Leaflet classes, making it transparent and driven by the chosen CRS. They make using Leaflet with custom projections (including flat maps) much easier, and remove the need for ugly hacks in the \+[Proj4\+Leaflet]\+(\href{https://github.com/kartena/Proj4Leaflet}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+kartena/\+\+Proj4\+Leaflet}}) plugin.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added \`{}\+CRS.Earth\`{} which serves as a base for all Earth-\/based CRS (\`{}\+EPSG3857\`{} etc.). \+[\#2345]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2345}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2345}})
\item Added \`{}\+Projection\`{} \`{}bounds\`{} property that defines bounds for different projections (\`{}\+Mercator\`{}, etc.) in projected coordinates (by \+[@perliedman]\+(\href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+perliedman}})).
\item Added \`{}\+CRS\`{} \`{}wrap\+Lat\`{} and \`{}wrap\+Lng\`{} properties which define whether the world wraps on a given axis and in what range. Set as \`{}\+[-\/180, 180]\+\`{} for \`{}\+EPSG:\+3857\`{}, \`{}\+EPSG:\+4326\`{}, \`{}\+EPSG:\+3395\`{} by default.
\item Added \`{}\+CRS\`{} and \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}wrap\+Lat\+Lng\`{} (the latter depends on the chosen CRS).
\item Added \`{}\+CRS\`{} \`{}infinite\`{} property that disables boundaries (the world can go on infinitely in any direction), default for \`{}\+CRS.Simple\`{}.
\item Added \`{}\+CRS\`{} \`{}get\+Projected\+Bounds\`{} and \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}get\+Pixel\+World\+Bounds\`{} methods that returns world bounds in projected coordinates depending on zoom (derived from \`{}\+Projection\`{} \`{}bounds\`{}) (by \+[@perliedman]\+(\href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+perliedman}})).
\item Added \`{}\+CRS\`{} \`{}unproject\`{} method that converts coordinates in CRS-\/dependent units into \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\`{} coordinates (by \+[@sowelie]\+(\href{https://github.com/sowelie}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+sowelie}})).
\item Added \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}distance(latlng1, latlng2)\`{} method that takes CRS into account and works with flat projections. \+[\#2345]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2345}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2345}}) \+[\#1442]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1442}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1442}})
\item Improved \`{}\+Circle\`{} to be approximated with an ellipse in Earth-\/based projections. \+[\#2345]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2345}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2345}})
\item Fixed \`{}\+EPSG:\+4326\`{} to have correct tile pyramid (2x1 tiles at root).
\item Fixed \`{}\+Projection.Spherical\+Mercator\`{} to project to meter units (by \+[@calvinmetcalf]\+(\href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+calvinmetcalf}})).
\item Fixed \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}world\+Copy\+Jump\`{} option to work for other projections.
\item Fixed \`{}\+Circle\`{} to work with flat projections. \+[\#2345]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2345}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2345}}) \+[\#1465]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1465}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1465}})
\item Fixed scale control precision in non-\/\+EPSG:\+3857 projections. \+[\#2345]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2345}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2345}})
\item Fixed \`{}\+Image\+Overlay\`{} not working properly in some non-\/standard projections. \+[\#3011]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3011}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3011}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1628}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Animations improvements and fractional zoom}{Animations improvements and fractional zoom}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1628}
Animation code in Leaflet had undergone a major rewrite (main PR:\+ \+[\#2382]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2382}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2382}})), bringing improvements such as:\+


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Multi-\/level tile buffering for more seamless zooming experience with less flickering
\item Optimal path animation (\`{}map.fly\+To\`{}) for zooming to a particular place in a curve (simultaneously zooming and panning)
\item Fractional zoom support --- now you can do things like \`{}map.set\+Zoom(12.\+45)\`{} and it just works.
\item Layers now rely on \`{}zoom\`{} event in addition to \`{}viewreset\`{} for frame-\/by-\/frame zoom animations. \+[\#3278]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3278}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3278}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1629}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{UX improvements}{UX improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1629}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved panning inertia behavior so that there are no tearing during animation when panning around quickly. \+[\#2360]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2360}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2360}})
\item Improved inertial scrolling to have a nicer, more natural feel (by \+[@\+Rick\+Mohr]\+(\href{https://github.com/RickMohr}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Rick\+Mohr}})). \+[Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet\#3063]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3063}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3063}}) \+[\#3063]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3063}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3063}}) \+[\#3062]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3062}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3062}}) \+[\#2987]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2987}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2987}})
\item Added popup fade out animation.
\item Improved keyboard support to ignore keystrokes with modifier keys (Ctrl, Alt, Meta) to not interfere with OS shortcuts.
\item Made popup to close when pressing Escape (by \+[@snkashis]\+(\href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+snkashis}})). \+[\#951]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/951}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+951}}) \+[\#3000]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3000}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3000}})
\item Improved keyboard zoom to zoom by 3 levels if shift key is pressed (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#3024]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3024}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3024}})
\item Improved layers control to become scrollable when there are too many layers (by \+[@rowanwins]\+(\href{https://github.com/rowanwins}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+rowanwins}})). \+[\#3571]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3571}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3571}}) \+[\#3167]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3167}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3167}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1630}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Misc. performance improvements}{Misc. performance improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1630}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Significantly \+[improved]\+(\href{http://jsperf.com/leaflet-parsefloat-in-latlng/2}{\texttt{http:\+/\+/\+jsperf.\+com/\+leaflet-\/parsefloat-\/in-\/latlng/\+2}}) \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\`{} creation performance (8x).
\item Improved performance of layer objects construction.
\item Significantly improved \`{}\+Feature\+Group\`{} (and correspondingly \`{}\+Geo\+JSON\`{}) layer adding and events performance (about 10x) by implementing a much better event propagation mechanism. \+[\#2311]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2311}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2311}})
\item Improved Leaflet events and DOM events memory footprint.
\item Improved \`{}\+Evented\`{} \`{}off\`{} performance by about 2 times.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1631}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Other breaking API changes}{Other breaking API changes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1631}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}off\`{} to require \`{}context\`{} attribute if you remove a listener that was previously added with a particular context.
\item Removed \`{}\+Dom\+Util.get\+Viewport\+Offset\`{} method as it is no longer necessary.
\item Removed \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}get\+Translate\+String\`{} and \`{}get\+Scale\+String\`{} methods.
\item Removed \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}document\+Is\+Ltr\`{} method.
\item Removed \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\`{} \`{}\+RAD\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+DEG\`{}, \`{}\+DEG\+\_\+\+TO\+\_\+\+RAD\`{} and \`{}\+MAX\+\_\+\+MARGIN\`{} constants.
\item Renamed \`{}\+Util.limit\+Exec\+By\+Interval\`{} to \`{}\+Util.throttle\`{}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1632}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Other API improvements}{Other API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1632}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added \`{}\+Evented\`{} class that now many Leaflet classes inherit from (instead of mixing in events methods in each class), while keeping the old \`{}includes:\+ L.\+Mixin.\+Events\`{} syntax available. \+[\#2310]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2310}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2310}})
\item Improved \`{}\+Class\`{} \`{}options\`{} to be prototypically inherited instead of copied over in children classes, which leads to more efficient memory use, faster object construction times and ability to change parent options that get propagated to all children automatically (by \+[@jfirebaugh]\+(\href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+jfirebaugh}})). \+[\#2300]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2300}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2300}}) \+[\#2294]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2294}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2294}})
\item Added \`{}\{r\}\`{} variable to \`{}\+Tile\+Layer\`{} \`{}url\`{} for adding \`{}"{}@2x"{}\`{} prefix on Retina-\/enabled devices (by \+[@urbaniak]\+(\href{https://github.com/urbaniak}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+urbaniak}})). \+[\#2296]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2296}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2296}})
\item Added \`{}\+Point\`{} \`{}ceil\`{} method (by \+[@perliedman]\+(\href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+perliedman}})).
\item Added \`{}\+Util.wrap\+Num\`{} method for wrapping a number to lie in a certain range.
\item Improved \`{}L.bind\`{} to use native \`{}\+Function\`{} \`{}bind\`{} on modern browsers and prepend real arguments to bound ones.
\item Added \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\`{} \`{}equals\`{} second argument \`{}max\+Margin\`{}.
\item Added \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}set\+Class\`{} and \`{}get\+Class\`{} methods.
\item Improved \`{}\+Marker\`{} \`{}move\`{} event to include \`{}old\+Latlng\`{} (by \+[@danzel]\+(\href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+danzel}})). \+[\#2412]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2412}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2412}})
\item Added \`{}\+Marker\`{} \`{}mousemove\`{} event (by \+[@bullgare]\+(\href{https://github.com/bullgare}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+bullgare}})). \+[\#2798]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2798}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2798}})
\item Improved \`{}\+Dom\+Event\`{} \`{}on\`{}/\+\`{}off\`{} to accept space-\/separated events and object literals (\`{}\{type:\+ fn\}\`{}).
\item Added \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}to\+Front\`{} and \`{}to\+Back\`{} methods.
\item Added \`{}\+Evented\`{} \`{}listens\`{} as a shortcut to \`{}has\+Event\+Listeners\`{}.
\item Added optional support for center-\/oriented scroll for \`{}L.map\`{} option \`{}touch\+Zoom\`{} (by \+[@mtmail]\+(\href{https://github.com/mtmail}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+mtmail}})). \+[\#2527]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2527}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2527}})
\item Added \`{}get\+Element\`{} method to all layers that returns an associated DOM element.
\item Added \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\`{} \`{}clone\`{} method (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#3390]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3390}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3390}})
\item Added \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}set\+Min\+Zoom\`{} and \`{}set\+Max\+Zoom\`{} methods (by \+[@nathancahill]\+(\href{https://github.com/nathancahill}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+nathancahill}})). \+[\#3383]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3383}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3383}}) \+[\#3380]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3380}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3380}})
\item Added \`{}original\+Event\`{} to \`{}\+Map\`{} and \`{}\+Marker\`{} \`{}drag\`{} and \`{}move\`{} event data (by \+[@yohanboniface]\+(\href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+yohanboniface}})). \+[\#3264]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3264}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3264}})
\item Added \`{}\+Popup\`{} \`{}auto\+Close\`{} option (by \+[@jfirebaugh]\+(\href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+jfirebaugh}})). \+[\#3018]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3018}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3018}}) \+[\#2716]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2716}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2716}}) \+[\#1853]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1853}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1853}})
\item Added \`{}\+Control.Zoom\`{} \`{}enable\`{} and \`{}disable\`{} methods. \+[\#3172]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/3172}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+3172}})
\item Added an argument to \`{}L.Poly\+Util.\+clip\+Polygon\`{} that controls rounding (by \+[@aparshin]\+(\href{https://github.com/aparshin}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+aparshin}})). \+[\#2926]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2926}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2926}}) \+[\#2917]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2917}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2917}})

\item Improved \`{}L.Util.\+extend\`{} performance (by \+[@fab1an]\+(\href{https://github.com/fab1an}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+fab1an}})). \+[\#2746]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2746}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2746}})
\item Added \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}stop\`{} method for stopping panning or \`{}fly\+To\`{} animation.
\item Added \`{}\+Map\`{} \`{}max\+Bounds\+Viscosity\`{} option that controls how much the map resits dragging out of max bounds (set to \`{}1\`{} for a hard limit) (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})). \+[\#2224]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2224}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2224}}) \+[\#3510]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3510}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3510}}) \+[\#1673]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1673}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+1673}})
\item Added \`{}\+Bounds\`{} and \`{}\+Lat\+Lng\+Bounds\`{} \`{}overlaps\`{} method (by \+[@\+Ivan\+Sanchez]\+(\href{https://github.com/IvanSanchez}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Ivan\+Sanchez}})). \+[\#2981]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2981}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+issues/\+2981}}) \+[\#3508]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3508}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+3508}})

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1633}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bugfixes}{Bugfixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1633}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed \`{}\+Dom\+Util\`{} \`{}on\`{} to make it possible to add the same listener to the same element for multiple contexts.
\item Fixed a bug that thowed an error when attempting to reinitialize the map on unload (by \+[@gamb]\+(\href{https://github.com/gamb}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+gamb}})). \+[\#2410]\+(\href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2410}{\texttt{https:\+/\+/\+github.\+com/\+\+Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet/\+pull/\+2410}})
\item Fixed excessively blurry non-\/retina tiles on retina i\+OS devices.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved the build system ({\ttfamily jake build}) to report gzipped library size.
\item Added version name and commit number to Leaflet builds. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2276}{\texttt{\#2276}}
\item Added Leaflet logo in vector format as {\ttfamily src/\+images/\+logo.\+svg}.
\item Added reference to Leaflet CSS in {\ttfamily package.\+json} (by \href{https://github.com/bclinkinbeard}{\texttt{@bclinkinbeard}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2432}{\texttt{\#2432}}
\item Switched from JSHint to ESLint for checking code style and made the checks more strict. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/3176}{\texttt{\#3176}}
\item Added a plugin guide section on module loaders and publishing plugins (by \href{https://github.com/patrickarlt}{\texttt{@patrickarlt}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2955}{\texttt{\#2955}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2955}{\texttt{Leaflet/\+\+Leaflet\#2955}}
\item Fixed the build system to work in non-\/git Leaflet folder (by \href{https://github.com/cschwarz}{\texttt{@cschwarz}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2758}{\texttt{\#2758}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1635}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+7.\+7 (2015-\/10-\/26)}{0.\+7.\+7 (2015-\/10-\/26)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1635}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression that could sometimes cause tiles to disappear when pinch-\/zooming on i\+OS devices.

\item Fixed touch interactions in Edge browser (by @mitchless \& @\+Neorth). \#3853 \#3379
\item Fixed a bug where removing a layer group from a feature group would throw an error (by @\+Lambdac0re). \#3869
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added proper {\bfseries{bower}} and {\bfseries{component}} support (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2561}{\texttt{\#2561}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1903}{\texttt{\#1903}}
\item Fixed a bug where dragging the map outside the window caused an error on FF. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2610}{\texttt{\#2610}}
\item Fixed a bug where some taps on Android where not working, often falsely perceived as drags (by \href{https://github.com/axefrog}{\texttt{@axefrog}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2503}{\texttt{\#2503}}
\item Fixed a bug where clicks on Android were skipped when happened too fast. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2303}{\texttt{\#2303}}
\item Fixed a bug where calling {\ttfamily set\+View} (or similar methods) several times in succession could freeze the map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2521}{\texttt{\#2521}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2236}{\texttt{\#2236}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2485}{\texttt{\#2485}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} wasn\textquotesingle{}t properly removed (by \href{https://github.com/jack-kerouac}{\texttt{@jack-\/kerouac}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2569}{\texttt{\#2569}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily load} event not to fire properly. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2510}{\texttt{\#2510}}
\item Fixed Canvas-\/based paths not triggering {\ttfamily remove} event when removed (by @adimitrov). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2486}{\texttt{\#2486}}
\item Fixed a bug where you could end up with fractional zoom after pinch-\/zooming in some cases (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2400}{\texttt{\#2400}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1934}{\texttt{\#1943}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1639}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+7.\+2 (2014-\/01-\/17)}{0.\+7.\+2 (2014-\/01-\/17)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1639}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that appeared with {\bfseries{Chrome 32 update}} that made all {\bfseries{mouse events shifted on scrolled pages}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2352}{\texttt{\#2352}}
\item Fixed a bug that could break tile loading when using non-\/standard tile sizes. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2288}{\texttt{\#2288}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily max\+Native\+Zoom} option didn\textquotesingle{}t work with TMS tile layers (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2321}{\texttt{\#2321}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2314}{\texttt{\#2314}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1640}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+7.\+1 (2013-\/12-\/06)}{0.\+7.\+1 (2013-\/12-\/06)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1640}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where pinch-\/zooming quickly could occasionally leave the map at a fractional zoom thus breaking tile loading (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2269}{\texttt{\#2269}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2255}{\texttt{\#2255}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1934}{\texttt{\#1934}}
\item Fixed tile flickering issues on some old Android 2/\+3 devices by disabling buggy hardware accelerated CSS there (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2216}{\texttt{\#2216}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2198}{\texttt{\#2198}}
\item Fixed a regression that sometimes led to an error when you started pinch-\/zoom as the first action on the map (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2259}{\texttt{\#2259}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2256}{\texttt{\#2256}}
\item Reverted {\ttfamily L.\+Util.\+template} optimizations to allow Leaflet to be used in eval-\/banning environments like browser extensions (performance gain was insignificant anyway) (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2217}{\texttt{\#2217}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2209}{\texttt{\#2209}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1968}{\texttt{\#1968}}
\item Fixed a regression where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily invalidate\+Size} could lead to unexpected results when called before map initialization (by \href{https://github.com/Zverik}{\texttt{@Zverik}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2250}{\texttt{\#2250}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2249}{\texttt{\#2249}}
\item Fixed a regression where {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} containing other group overwrote original {\ttfamily e.\+layer} value in mouse events (by \href{https://github.com/gumballhead}{\texttt{@gumballhead}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2253}{\texttt{\#2253}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2252}{\texttt{\#2252}}
\item Fixed a regression where {\ttfamily Circle\+Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lngs} didn\textquotesingle{}t return {\ttfamily this} (by \href{https://github.com/radicalbiscuit}{\texttt{@radicalbiscuit}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2206}{\texttt{\#2206}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1641}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+7 (2013-\/11-\/18)}{0.\+7 (2013-\/11-\/18)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1641}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1642}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Improvements}{Improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1642}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1643}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usability improvements}{Usability improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1643}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{support for IE11 touch devices}} (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}, \href{https://github.com/DanielX2}{\texttt{@Daniel\+X2}} and \href{https://github.com/fnicollet}{\texttt{@fnicollet}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2039}{\texttt{\#2039}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2066}{\texttt{\#2066}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2037}{\texttt{\#2037}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2102}{\texttt{\#2102}}
\item Added shift-\/double-\/click to zoom out shortcut. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2185}{\texttt{\#2185}}
\item Significantly improved {\bfseries{controls design on mobile}} devices. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1868}{\texttt{\#1868}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2012}{\texttt{\#2012}}
\item Fixed and improved IE7-\/8 control and popup styles.
\item Made subtle improvements to control styles on desktop browsers.
\item Improved keyboard nav support so that map doesn\textquotesingle{}t loose focus when you click on a control (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2150}{\texttt{\#2150}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2148}{\texttt{\#2148}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily max\+Bounds} behavior:\+ now it doesn\textquotesingle{}t force higher minimal zoom, and anchors to max bounds edges properly when zooming (by \href{https://github.com/kapouer}{\texttt{@kapouer}} and \href{https://github.com/mourner}{\texttt{@mourner}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2187}{\texttt{\#2187}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1946}{\texttt{\#1946}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2081}{\texttt{\#2081}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2168}{\texttt{\#2168}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1908}{\texttt{\#1908}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1644}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Map API improvements}{Map API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1644}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Made {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily set\+View} {\ttfamily zoom} argument optional. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2056}{\texttt{\#2056}}
\item Added {\ttfamily max\+Zoom} option to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily fit\+Bounds}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2101}{\texttt{\#2101}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily bounce\+At\+Zoom\+Limits} option that makes the map bounce when you pinch-\/zoom past limits (it worked like this before, but now you can disable this) (by \href{https://github.com/trevorpowell}{\texttt{@trevorpowell}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1864}{\texttt{\#1864}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2072}{\texttt{\#2072}}
\item Added {\ttfamily distance} property to {\ttfamily Map} and {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily dragend} events. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2158}{\texttt{\#2158}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/872}{\texttt{\#872}}
\item Added optional support for center-\/oriented scroll and double-\/click zoom (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1939}{\texttt{\#1939}}
\item Added {\ttfamily timestamp} to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily locationfound} event. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/584}{\texttt{\#584}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily invalidate\+Size} to call {\ttfamily moveend} immediately unless given {\ttfamily debounce\+Moveend:\+ true} option (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2181}{\texttt{\#2181}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1645}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Tile\+Layer API improvements}{Tile\+Layer API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1645}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily max\+Native\+Zoom} option that allows displaying tile layers on zoom levels above their maximum by {\bfseries{upscaling tiles}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1802}{\texttt{\#1802}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1798}{\texttt{\#1798}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily tileloadstart} event (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2142}{\texttt{\#2142}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2140}{\texttt{\#2140}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} world size (used for wrapping and limiting tiles) to be derived from CRS instead of hardcoded, making it easier to use with custom projections (by \href{https://github.com/perliedman}{\texttt{@perliedman}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2160}{\texttt{\#2160}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added an \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/blob/main/FAQ.md}{\texttt{official FAQ}}.
\item Cleaned up and moved old IE styles to {\ttfamily leaflet.\+css} and removed {\ttfamily leaflet.\+ie.\+css}, so {\bfseries{no need for IE conditional comment}} when including Leaflet now. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2159}{\texttt{\#2159}}

\item Officially {\bfseries{dropped support for IE6}}. Nobody cares anyway, and Leaflet should still be accessible on it. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2159}{\texttt{\#2159}}
\item Improved the build system to check JS errors in spec files. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2151}{\texttt{\#2151}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily jake} command to run tests before building the source. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2151}{\texttt{\#2151}}
\item Switched the main file in {\ttfamily package.\+json} to unminified version for NPM/\+\+Browserify (by \href{https://github.com/icetan}{\texttt{@icetan}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2109}{\texttt{\#2109}}

\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1652}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+6 regression fixes}{0.\+6 regression fixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1652}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a {\bfseries{memory leak in i\+OS7}} that could crash Safari when handling lots of objects (e.\+g. 1000 markers) (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/2149}{\texttt{\#2149}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2122}{\texttt{\#2122}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused lag at the beginning of panning in Chrome (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2163}{\texttt{\#2163}}
\item Fixed a regression that made the layers control unscrollable in Firefox. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2029}{\texttt{\#2029}}
\item Fixed a regression that broke {\ttfamily world\+Copy\+Jump:\+ true} option (by \href{https://github.com/fastrde}{\texttt{@fastrde}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1904}{\texttt{\#1904}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1831}{\texttt{\#1831}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1982}{\texttt{\#1982}}
\item Fixed a regression where a first map click after popup close button click was ignored (by \href{https://github.com/fastrde}{\texttt{@fastrde}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1537}{\texttt{\#1537}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1963}{\texttt{\#1963}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1925}{\texttt{\#1925}}
\item Fixed a regression where {\ttfamily L.\+Dom\+Util.\+get\+Mouse\+Position} would throw an error if container argument not provided (by \href{https://github.com/scooterw}{\texttt{@scooterw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1826}{\texttt{\#1826}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1928}{\texttt{\#1928}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1926}{\texttt{\#1926}}
\item Fixed a regression with vector layers positioning when zooming on IE10+ touch devices (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2002}{\texttt{\#2002}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2000}{\texttt{\#2000}}
\item Fixed a regression with {\ttfamily max\+Bounds} behaving weirdly on panning inertia out of bounds. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2168}{\texttt{\#2168}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1653}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{General bugfixes}{General bugfixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1653}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where the map could freeze if centered and immediately recentered on initialization. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2071}{\texttt{\#2071}}
\item Fixed a bug where all maps except the first one on a page didn\textquotesingle{}t track window resize. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1980}{\texttt{\#1980}}
\item Fixed a bug where tiles in {\ttfamily EPSG:\+3395} projection were shifted (by \href{https://github.com/aparshin}{\texttt{@aparshin}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2020}{\texttt{\#2020}}
\item Fixed a bug where scale control displayed wrong scale when on pages with {\ttfamily box-\/sizing:\+ border-\/box}.
\item Fixed a bug where zoom control button didn\textquotesingle{}t appear as disabled if map was initialized at the zoom limit. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2083}{\texttt{\#2083}}
\item Fixed a bug where box zoom also triggered a map click event (by \href{https://github.com/fastrde}{\texttt{@fastrde}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1951}{\texttt{\#1951}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1884}{\texttt{\#1884}}
\item Fixed a bug where shift-\/clicking on a map immediately after a drag didn\textquotesingle{}t trigger a click event (by \href{https://github.com/fastrde}{\texttt{@fastrde}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1952}{\texttt{\#1952}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1950}{\texttt{\#1950}}
\item Fixed a bug where content was updated twice when opening a popup. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/2137}{\texttt{\#2137}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item Fixed a regression where the map would stuck when trying to animate zoom before any tile layers are added to the map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1484}{\texttt{\#1484}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1845}{\texttt{\#1845}}
\item Fixed a regression with the layers control and popups closing on inside click in IE \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 9. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1850}{\texttt{\#1850}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed vector feature flickering on Safari Mac for screen \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 2000px. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/902}{\texttt{\#902}}

\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily min\+Zoom} and {\ttfamily max\+Zoom} didn\textquotesingle{}t always override values derived from the added tile layers. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1848}{\texttt{1848}}

\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} still fired {\ttfamily layerremove} event on {\ttfamily remove\+Layer} even if the given layer wan\textquotesingle{}t present in the group (by (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}})). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1847}{\texttt{\#1847}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1858}{\texttt{\#1858}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Opacity} wasn\textquotesingle{}t returning the marker (by \href{https://github.com/freepius44}{\texttt{@freepius44}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1851}{\texttt{\#1851}}
\item Fixed a bug where removing the map element from the DOM before panning transition has finished could keep a set\+Interval loop running forever (by \href{https://github.com/rutkovsky}{\texttt{@rutkovsky}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1825}{\texttt{\#1825}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1856}{\texttt{\#1856}}
\item Fixed mobile styles to apply to {\ttfamily leaflet-\/bar} elements.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added ability to pass zoom/\+pan animation options to {\ttfamily set\+Max\+Bounds} (by \href{http://git.io/djb}{\texttt{@davidjb}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1834}{\texttt{\#1834}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Leaflet builds (\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.js files in the {\ttfamily dist} folder) were removed from the repo and are now done automatically on each commit for {\ttfamily master} and {\ttfamily stable} branches by \href{travis-ci.org/Leaflet/Leaflet}{\texttt{Travis CI}}. The download links are on the \href{http://leafletjs.com/download.html}{\texttt{Leaflet download page}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1665}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+6.\+2 (2013-\/06-\/28)}{0.\+6.\+2 (2013-\/06-\/28)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1665}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that caused wrong tile layers stacking order when using opacity \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 1 (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1804}{\texttt{\#1804}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1790}{\texttt{\#1790}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1667}{\texttt{\#1667}}
\item Fixed a regression that caused tiles selection when double-\/clicking absolutely positioned maps with vector layers in it in Firefox (WTF!) (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1807}{\texttt{\#1807}}
\item Fixed a regression with a wrong cursor when dragging a map with vector layers, and tiles becoming selected on double click (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1800}{\texttt{\#1800}}
\item Fixed a regression that caused flickering of tiles near map border on zoom animation in Chrome.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1666}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+6.\+1 (2013-\/06-\/27)}{0.\+6.\+1 (2013-\/06-\/27)}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1666}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression with mouse wheel zooming too fast on Firefox (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1788}{\texttt{\#1788}}
