\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1668}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking changes}{Breaking changes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1668}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Moved polyline editing code into \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet.draw}{\texttt{Leaflet.\+draw}} plugin (where it fits much better along with all other editing and drawing handlers). The API remains the same.
\item Dropped support for environments that augment {\ttfamily Object.\+prototype} (luckily it\textquotesingle{}s a thing of the past nowadays).
\item {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily invalidate\+Size} no longer fires {\ttfamily move} and {\ttfamily moveend} events if the map size didn\textquotesingle{}t change. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1819}{\texttt{\#1819}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1669}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Improvements}{Improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1669}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1670}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Usability and performance improvements}{Usability and performance improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1670}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Improved zoom control design}} -\/ cleaner, simpler, more accessible (mostly by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1313}{\texttt{\#1313}}
\item Updated {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} icon (designed by Volker Kinkelin), added retina version and SVG source. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1739}{\texttt{\#1739}}
\item Added keyboard accessibility to markers (you can now tab to them and press enter for click behavior). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1355}{\texttt{\#1355}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} zoom animation to eliminate flickering in case one tile layer on top of another or when zooming several times quickly (by \href{https://github.com/mourner}{\texttt{@mourner}} with lots of fixes from \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1140}{\texttt{\#1140}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1437}{\texttt{\#1437}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/52}{\texttt{\#52}}
\item Subtly improved default popup styles
\item Improved attribution control to be much less obtrusive (no "{}powered by"{}, just a Leaflet link). You can still remove the prefix with {\ttfamily map.\+attribution\+Control.\+set\+Prefix(\textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{})} if you need.
\item Improved zoom behavior so that there\textquotesingle{}s no drift of coordinates when you change zoom back and forth without panning. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/426}{\texttt{\#426}}
\item Improved double click behavior to zoom while keeping the clicked point fixed (by \href{https://github.com/ansis}{\texttt{@ansis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1582}{\texttt{\#1582}}
\item Improved dragging behavior to not get stuck if mouse moved outside of an iframe containing the map (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1277}{\texttt{\#1277}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1782}{\texttt{\#1782}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1786}{\texttt{\#1786}}
\item Improved box zoom to be cancelable by pressing Escape (by \href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{@yohanboniface}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1438}{\texttt{\#1438}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Marker} popups to close on marker click if opened (by \href{https://github.com/popox}{\texttt{@popox}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1761}{\texttt{\#1761}}
\item Significantly improved mass layer removal performance (by \href{https://github.com/jfgirard}{\texttt{@jfgirard}} with fixes from \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1141}{\texttt{\#1141}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1514}{\texttt{\#1514}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1671}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{API improvements}{API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1671}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1672}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Layers API improvements}{Layers API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1672}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily to\+Geo\+JSON} method to various layer types, allowing you to {\bfseries{save your Leaflet layers as Geo\+JSON}}. (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1462}{\texttt{\#1462}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/712}{\texttt{\#712}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1779}{\texttt{\#1779}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily coords\+To\+Lat\+Lng} option for dealing with Geo\+JSON that has non-\/\+WGS84 coords (thanks to \href{https://github.com/moonlite}{\texttt{@moonlite}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/888}{\texttt{\#888}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/886}{\texttt{\#886}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Marker} to reuse icon DOM elements when changing icons on the fly (e.\+g. fixes problems when changing icon on mouse hover) (by \href{https://github.com/robpvn}{\texttt{@robpvn}} \& \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1726}{\texttt{\#1726}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/561}{\texttt{\#561}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1753}{\texttt{\#1753}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1754}{\texttt{\#1754}}
\item Added {\ttfamily latlng} property to {\ttfamily Marker} mouse event data. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1613}{\texttt{\#1613}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily has\+Layer} method (by \href{https://github.com/rvlasveld}{\texttt{@rvlasveld}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1282}{\texttt{\#1282}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1300}{\texttt{\#1300}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily get\+Layers} method (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1469}{\texttt{\#1469}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily get\+Layer} method (by \href{https://github.com/gumballhead}{\texttt{@gumballhead}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1650}{\texttt{\#1650}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily remove\+Layer} method to also accept layer {\ttfamily id} (by \href{https://github.com/gumballhead}{\texttt{@gumballhead}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1642}{\texttt{\#1642}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Path} {\ttfamily pointer\+Events} option for setting pointer-\/events on SVG-\/powered vector layers (by \href{https://github.com/inpursuit}{\texttt{@inpursuit}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1053}{\texttt{\#1053}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Polygon} to filter out last point if it\textquotesingle{}s equal to the first one (to fix Geo\+JSON polygon issues) (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1153}{\texttt{\#1153}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1135}{\texttt{\#1135}}
\item Improved paths with {\ttfamily clickable:\+ false} to allow mouse events to pass through to objects underneath (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1384}{\texttt{\#1384}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1281}{\texttt{\#1281}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily L.\+Util.\+template} (and correspondingly url-\/related {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} options) to support functions for data values (by \href{https://github.com/olegsmith}{\texttt{@olegsmith}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1554}{\texttt{\#1554}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily get\+Container} method (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1433}{\texttt{\#1433}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+Canvas} {\ttfamily redraw} method chaining (by \href{https://github.com/jieter}{\texttt{@jieter}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1287}{\texttt{\#1287}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} {\ttfamily crs} option to be able to use WMS of CRS other than the map CRS (by \href{https://github.com/kengu}{\texttt{@kengu}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/942}{\texttt{\#942}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/945}{\texttt{\#945}}
\item Added {\ttfamily popupopen} and {\ttfamily popupclose} events to various layers (by \href{https://github.com/Koc}{\texttt{@Koc}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/738}{\texttt{\#738}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily keep\+In\+View} option (thanks to \href{https://github.com/lapo-luchini}{\texttt{@lapo-\/luchini}}) that prevents the popup from going off-\/screen while it\textquotesingle{}s opened. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1308}{\texttt{\#1308}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1052}{\texttt{\#1052}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily toggle\+Popup} method (by \href{https://github.com/popox}{\texttt{@popox}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1761}{\texttt{\#1761}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily close\+On\+Click} option that overrides the same {\ttfamily Map} option for specific popups (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1669}{\texttt{\#1669}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Marker} and {\ttfamily Path} {\ttfamily bind\+Popup} method to also accept {\ttfamily Popup} objects (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1385}{\texttt{\#1385}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1208}{\texttt{\#1208}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1402}{\texttt{\#1402}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Popup\+Content} method (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1373}{\texttt{\#1373}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1673}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Map API improvements}{Map API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1673}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved all view changing methods of {\ttfamily Map} ({\ttfamily set\+View}, {\ttfamily pan\+To}, {\ttfamily set\+Zoom}, {\ttfamily fit\+Bounds}, etc.) to accept an options object, including the ability to precisely control zoom/\+pan animations they cause (force disable/\+enable, etc.). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1617}{\texttt{\#1617}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1616}{\texttt{\#1616}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/340}{\texttt{\#340}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/483}{\texttt{\#483}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1164}{\texttt{\#1164}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1420}{\texttt{\#1420}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily fit\+Bounds} method to accept {\ttfamily padding} (or {\ttfamily padding\+Top\+Left} and {\ttfamily padding\+Bottom\+Right}) options, allowing you to zoom to an area with a certain padding in pixels (usually left for controls). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/859}{\texttt{\#859}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily invalidate\+Size} to accept options object ({\ttfamily animate} and {\ttfamily pan}, the latter controls if it pans the map on size change). (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}} and \href{https://github.com/mourner}{\texttt{@mourner}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1766}{\texttt{\#1766}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1767}{\texttt{\#1767}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily set\+Zoom\+Around} method for zooming while keeping a certain point fixed (used by scroll and double-\/click zooming). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1157}{\texttt{\#1157}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily remove} method to properly destroy the map and clean up all events, and added corresponding {\ttfamily unload} event (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}} and \href{https://github.com/mourner}{\texttt{@mourner}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1434}{\texttt{\#1434}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1101}{\texttt{\#1101}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1621}{\texttt{\#1621}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily tap} handler that now contains all mobile hacks for enabling quick taps and long holds and {\ttfamily tap\+Tolerance} option specifying the number of pixels you can shift your finger for click to still fire.
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily zoom\+Animation\+Threshold} for setting the max zoom difference with which zoom animation can occur. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1377}{\texttt{\#1377}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily open\+Popup} method to also accept {\ttfamily (content, latlng)} signature as a shortcut.
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily close\+Popup} method to optionally accept a popup object to close. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1641}{\texttt{\#1641}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily stop\+Locate} method to abort resetting map view if calling {\ttfamily locate} with {\ttfamily set\+View} option. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/747}{\texttt{\#747}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} to throw exception if the specified container id is not found (by \href{htts://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1574}{\texttt{\#1574}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily locationfound} event to pass all location data (heading, speed, etc.). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/984}{\texttt{\#984}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/584}{\texttt{\#584}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/987}{\texttt{\#987}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1028}{\texttt{\#1028}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily resize} event. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1564}{\texttt{\#1564}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily zoomlevelschange} event that triggers when the current zoom range (min/\+max) changes (by \href{https://github.com/moonlite}{\texttt{@moonlite}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1376}{\texttt{\#1376}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1674}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Controls API improvements}{Controls API improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1674}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{generic toolbar classes}} for reuse by plugin developers (used by zoom control).
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily baselayerchange}, {\ttfamily overlayadd} and {\ttfamily overlayremove} events fired by {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}} and \href{https://github.com/Xelio}{\texttt{@Xelio}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1286}{\texttt{\#1286}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1634}{\texttt{\#1634}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Made Leaflet classes compatible with {\bfseries{Coffee\+Script class inheritance}} syntax (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1345}{\texttt{\#1345}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1314}{\texttt{\#1314}}
\item Added {\ttfamily clean\+All\+Event\+Listeners} method (aliased to {\ttfamily off} without arguments) to all events-\/enabled objects (by \href{https://github.com/iirvine}{\texttt{@iirvine}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1599}{\texttt{\#1599}}
\item Added {\ttfamily add\+One\+Time\+Event\+Listener} method (aliased to {\ttfamily once}) to all events-\/enabled objects (by \href{https://github.com/iirvine}{\texttt{@iirvine}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/473}{\texttt{\#473}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1596}{\texttt{\#1596}}
\item Added ability to pass coordinates as simple objects ({\ttfamily \{lat:\+ 50, lon:\+ 30\}} or {\ttfamily \{lat:\+ 50, lng:\+ 30\}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1412}{\texttt{\#1412}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily get\+North}, {\ttfamily get\+East}, {\ttfamily get\+South}, {\ttfamily get\+West} methods (by \href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{@yohanboniface}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1318}{\texttt{\#1318}}
\item Added {\ttfamily AMD} support (Leaflet now registers itself as a {\ttfamily leaflet} AMD module) (with fixes from \href{https://github.com/sheppard}{\texttt{@sheppard}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1364}{\texttt{\#1364}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1778}{\texttt{\#1778}}
\item Added {\ttfamily L.\+Util.\+trim} function (by \href{https://github.com/kristerkari}{\texttt{@kristerkari}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1607}{\texttt{\#1607}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1676}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Development workflow improvements}{Development workflow improvements}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1676}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Switched from Jasmine to \href{http://visionmedia.github.io/mocha/}{\texttt{Mocha}} with Expect.\+js (matchers) and Sinon (spies) for tests (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}} \& \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1479}{\texttt{\#1479}}
\item Added \href{http://karma-runner.github.io}{\texttt{Karma}} integration for running tests in a headless Phantom\+JS instance and code coverage reporting (by \href{https://github.com/edjafarov}{\texttt{@edjafarov}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1326}{\texttt{\#1326}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1340}{\texttt{\#1340}}
\item Added \href{https://travis-ci.org/Leaflet/Leaflet}{\texttt{Travis CI integration}} for linting and running tests for each commit and pull request automatically (by \href{https://github.com/edjafarov}{\texttt{@edjafarov}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1336}{\texttt{\#1336}}
\item Significantly improved test coverage
\item Added compatibility with lazy evaluation scripts (by \href{https://github.com/kristerkari}{\texttt{@kristerkari}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1288}{\texttt{\#1288}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1607}{\texttt{\#1607}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1288}{\texttt{\#1288}}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1677}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bugfixes}{Bugfixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1677}
\hypertarget{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1678}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{General bugfixes}{General bugfixes}}\label{md_frontend_2node__modules_2leaflet_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md1678}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed lots of issues with extent restriction by {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily max\+Bounds}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1491}{\texttt{\#1491}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1475}{\texttt{\#1475}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1194}{\texttt{\#1194}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/900}{\texttt{\#900}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1333}{\texttt{\#1333}}
\item Fixed occasional crashes by disabling zoom animation if changing zoom level by more than 4 levels. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1377}{\texttt{\#1377}}
\item Fixed a bug with that caused stuttery keyboard panning in some cases (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1710}{\texttt{\#1710}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused unwanted scrolling of the page to the top of the map on focus. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1228}{\texttt{\#1228}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1540}{\texttt{\#1540}}
\item Fixed a bug where clicking on a marker with an open popup caused the popup to faded in again (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/560}{\texttt{\#506}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1386}{\texttt{\#1386}}
\item Fixed a bug where zoom buttons disabled state didn\textquotesingle{}t update on min/\+max zoom change (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1372}{\texttt{\#1372}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1328}{\texttt{\#1328}}
\item Fixed a bug where scrolling slightly wouldn\textquotesingle{}t always zoom out the map (by \href{https://github.com/cschwarz}{\texttt{@cschwarz}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1575}{\texttt{\#1575}}
\item Fixed popup close button to not leave an outline after clicking on it and reopening the popup (by \href{https://github.com/dotCypress}{\texttt{@dot\+Cypress}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1537}{\texttt{\#1537}}
\item Fixed a bug that prevented tiles from loading during pan animation.
\item Fixed a bug with {\ttfamily contextmenu} events on popups falling through to map (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1730}{\texttt{\#1730}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1732}{\texttt{\#1732}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily 404} tile loading errors when browsing the map off the world bounds.
\item Fixed shifted mouse events in some cases with map inside a relatively positioned parent (by \href{https://github.com/scooterw}{\texttt{@scooterw}} and \href{https://github.com/jec006}{\texttt{@jec006}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1670}{\texttt{\#1670}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1684}{\texttt{\#1684}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1745}{\texttt{\#1745}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1744}{\texttt{\#1744}}
\item Fixed a bug where tile layer z-\/index order sometimes broke after view reset. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1422}{\texttt{\#1422}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug with undesirable page scrolling in Firefox 17+ when you zoom the map by scrolling (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1789}{\texttt{\#1789}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1788}{\texttt{\#1788}}
\item Fixed a bug where mouse coordinates where shifted in Firefox if the map was inside a positioned block on a scrolled page (by \href{https://github.com/joschka}{\texttt{@joschka}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1365}{\texttt{\#1365}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1322}{\texttt{\#1322}}
\item Fixed a bug where box zoom didn\textquotesingle{}t work in some cases in Firefox 18+ (by \href{https://github.com/fabriceds}{\texttt{@fabriceds}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1405}{\texttt{\#1405}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} opacity didn\textquotesingle{}t work in IE 7-\/8 (by \href{https://github.com/javisantana}{\texttt{@javisantana}} \& \href{https://gi.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1084}{\texttt{\#1084}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1396}{\texttt{\#1396}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1371}{\texttt{\#1371}}
\item Fixed Leaflet not working correctly in Phantom\+JS (by \href{https://github.com/rassie}{\texttt{@rassie}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1501}{\texttt{\#1501}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Mobile bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug with layers control on Win\+Phone8/\+\+IE10 Touch (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1635}{\texttt{\#1635}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1539}{\texttt{\#1539}}
\item Fixed a bug with click sometimes firing twice on Win\+Phone8/\+\+IE10 Touch (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1694}{\texttt{\#1694}}
\item Fixed a bug in Android where click was triggered twice on one tap (by \href{https://github.com/jerel}{\texttt{@jerel}} \& \href{https://github.com/mourner}{\texttt{@mourner}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1227}{\texttt{\#1227}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1263}{\texttt{\#1263}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1785}{\texttt{\#1785}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1694}{\texttt{\#1694}}
\item Fixed a bug in Android where click on a collapsed layers control would immediately select one of the layers (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1784}{\texttt{\#1784}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1694}{\texttt{\#1694}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API bugfixes

\#\#\#\#\# General API bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed click mouse event inside popups {\bfseries{not propagating outside the map}} (fixes issues with j\+Query.\+live and some mobile frameworks that rely on document click listeners). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/301}{\texttt{\#301}}
\item Fixed a bug where event listener still fired even if it was removed on the same event in other listener (by \href{https://github.com/spamdaemon}{\texttt{@spamdaemon}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1661}{\texttt{\#1661}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1654}{\texttt{\#1654}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily L.\+point} and {\ttfamily L.\+lat\+Lng} factories weren\textquotesingle{}t passing {\ttfamily null} and {\ttfamily undefined} values through.
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Dom\+Event} {\ttfamily remove\+Listener} function chaining (by \href{https://github.com/pagameba}{\texttt{@pagameba}}).
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily remove\+Event\+Listener} would throw an error if no events are registered on the object (by \href{https://github.com/tjoekbezoer}{\texttt{@tjoekbezoer}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1632}{\texttt{\#1632}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1631}{\texttt{\#1631}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Point} {\ttfamily equals} and {\ttfamily contains} methods didn\textquotesingle{}t accept points in array form.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily extend} of an undefined object would cause an error (by \href{https://github.com/korzhyk}{\texttt{@korzhyk}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1688}{\texttt{\#1688}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Control.\+Attribution} {\ttfamily remove\+Attribution} of inexistant attribution corrupted the attribution text. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1410}{\texttt{\#1410}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily set\+View} on an invisible map caused an error (by \href{https://github.com/jfire}{\texttt{@jfire}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1707}{\texttt{\#1707}}
\item Fixed compatibility with Browserify (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1572}{\texttt{\#1572}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\#\# Layers API bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where default marker icon path wasn\textquotesingle{}t properly detected in some cases in IE6-\/7 (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1294}{\texttt{\#1294}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} param values weren\textquotesingle{}t escaped in URLs (by \href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{@yohanboniface}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1317}{\texttt{\#1317}}
\item Fixed a bug where layers that belong to multiple feature groups didn\textquotesingle{}t propagate events correctly (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1359}{\texttt{\#1359}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} {\ttfamily tile\+Size} option was ignored (by \href{https://github.com/brianhatchl}{\texttt{@brianhatchl}}). \href{https://github.com/brianhatchl}{\texttt{\#1080}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Polyline} constructor could overwrite the source array (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}} and \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1439}{\texttt{\#1439}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1092}{\texttt{\#1092}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1246}{\texttt{\#1246}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1426}{\texttt{\#1426}}
\item Fixed a bug where marker dragging disabling/\+enabling wouldn\textquotesingle{}t always work correctly (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}} and \href{https://github.com/escaped}{\texttt{@escaped}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1471}{\texttt{\#1471}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1551}{\texttt{\#1551}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} to prevent incorrect subdomain in case of negative tile coordinates (by \href{https://github.com/malexeev}{\texttt{@malexeev}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1532}{\texttt{\#1532}}
\item Fixed polygons to normalize holes (remove last point if it\textquotesingle{}s equal to the first one) (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1467}{\texttt{\#}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1459}{\texttt{\#1459}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Div\+Icon} {\ttfamily html} option to accept {\ttfamily 0} as a value (by \href{https://github.com/stuporglue}{\texttt{@stuporglue}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1633}{\texttt{\#1633}}
\item Fixed a bug with Canvas-\/based paths throwing an error on {\ttfamily mousemove} in certain conditions. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1615}{\texttt{\#1615}}
\item Fixed a bug where copies of the world wouldn\textquotesingle{}t load if you set {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily bounds} (by \href{https://github.com/ansis}{\texttt{@ansis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1618}{\texttt{\#1618}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily load} event wouldn\textquotesingle{}t always fire correctly. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1565}{\texttt{\#1565}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} compatibility with some old servers that only accepted request parameters in uppercase. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1751}{\texttt{\#1751}}
\item Fixed a bug with incorrect {\ttfamily L.\+Icon.\+Default.\+image\+Path} detection in some cases. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1657}{\texttt{\#1657}}
\item Fixed a bug where layer {\ttfamily on\+Remove} was still called even if it was never added (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1729}{\texttt{\#1729}}
\item Fixed a bug where calling {\ttfamily set\+Radius} on a Canvas-\/powered {\ttfamily Circle\+Marker} would cause an infinite loop (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1712}{\texttt{\#1712}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1713}{\texttt{\#1713}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1728}{\texttt{\#1728}}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily marker-\/icon@2x.\+png} to {\ttfamily marker-\/icon-\/2x.\+png} to fix compatibility with Google App\+Engine. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1552}{\texttt{\#1552}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1553}{\texttt{\#1553}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily popupclose} and {\ttfamily popupopen} events weren\textquotesingle{}t fired for multipolygons and multipolylines (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1681}{\texttt{\#1681}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\#\# Map API bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily fit\+Bounds} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work correctly with large bounds (thanks to \href{https://github.com/MaZderMind}{\texttt{@Ma\+Zder\+Mind}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1069}{\texttt{\#1069}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily has\+Layer} wasn\textquotesingle{}t handling {\ttfamily null} objects (by \href{https://github.com/rvlasveld}{\texttt{@rvlasveld}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1282}{\texttt{\#1282}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1302}{\texttt{\#1302}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily moveend} fired before {\ttfamily dragend} on drag (by \href{https://github.com/oslek}{\texttt{@oslek}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1374}{\texttt{\#1374}}
\item Fixed a bug where panning with inertia produced an excessive {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily movestart} event on inertia start (by \href{https://github.com/oslek}{\texttt{@oslek}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1374}{\texttt{\#1374}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily moveend} fired repeatedly on window resize even if the actual map size didn\textquotesingle{}t change (by \href{https://github.com/oslek}{\texttt{@oslek}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1374}{\texttt{\#1374}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily moveend} sometimes wasn\textquotesingle{}t fired after drag (particularly often when dragging with a trackpad).
\item Fixed a bug that would cause an error when trying to get the state of the map in a {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily load} event listener. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/962}{\texttt{\#962}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily autopanstart} event back (it was removed occasionally in previous version). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1375}{\texttt{\#1375}}
\item Fixed a bug with removing previously set {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily max\+Bounds} (by \href{https://github.com/jec006}{\texttt{@jec006}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1749}{\texttt{\#1749}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1750}{\texttt{\#1750}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+5.\+1 (2013-\/02-\/06)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression with {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} not accepting arrays of {\ttfamily Feature\+Collection} (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1299}{\texttt{\#1299}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1298}{\texttt{\#1298}}
\item Fixed a regression with {\ttfamily Cirle\+Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Radius} not working if called before adding the layer to the map (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1342}{\texttt{\#1342}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1297}{\texttt{\#1297}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+5 (2013-\/01-\/17)

\#\#\# Breaking changes

Be sure to read through these changes to avoid any issues when upgrading from older versions:\+


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Removed default {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} wrapping/\+clamping of coordinates ({\ttfamily -\/180, -\/90} to {\ttfamily 180, 90}), wrapping moved to an explicit method ({\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} {\ttfamily wrap}).
\item Disabled {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily world\+Copy\+Jump} option by default (jumping back to the original world copy when panning out of it). Enable it explicitly if you need it.
\item Changed styles for the zoom control (you may need to update your custom styles for it).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Improvements

\#\#\#\# Usability improvements

\#\#\#\#\# Interaction


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added touch zoom, pan and double tap support for {\bfseries{IE10 touch devices and Metro apps}} (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}} and \href{https://github.com/veproza}{\texttt{@veproza}} with help from \href{https://github.com/oliverheilig}{\texttt{@oliverheilig}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1076}{\texttt{\#1076}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/871}{\texttt{\#871}}
\item {\bfseries{Improved panning inertia}} to be much more natural and smooth.
\item {\bfseries{Improved dragging cursors}} in Chrome, Safari and Firefox (now grabbing hand cursors are used).
\item Improved zoom animation curve for a better feel overall.
\item Improved scroll wheel zoom to be more responsive.
\item Improved panning animation performance in IE6-\/8.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\#\# Controls


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Improved zoom control design}} to look better, more neutral and in line with other controls, making it easier to customize and fit different website designs. Replaced +/\+-\/ images with text.
\item Improved zoom control to zoom by 3 levels if you hold shift while clicking on a button.
\item Improved zoom control buttons to become visually disabled when min/\+max zoom is reached. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/917}{\texttt{\#917}}
\item Improved scale control styles.
\item Improved fallback control styles for IE6-\/8.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\#\# Other


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{retina support for markers}} (through {\ttfamily Icon} {\ttfamily icon\+Retina\+Url} and {\ttfamily shadow\+Retina\+Url} options) (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1048}{\texttt{\#1048}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1174}{\texttt{\#1174}}
\item Added retina-\/sized default marker icon in addition to standard one (along with its SVG source and with some subtle design improvements) (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1048}{\texttt{\#1048}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1174}{\texttt{\#1174}}
\item Improved vectors updating/\+removing performance on Canvas backend (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/961}{\texttt{\#961}}
\item Cut total images size from 10KB to 3.\+2\+KB with \href{http://www.smushit.com/ysmush.it/}{\texttt{Yahoo Smush.\+it}}. Thanks to Peter Rounce for suggestion.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Replaced {\ttfamily L.\+Transition} with a much better and simpler {\ttfamily L.\+Pos\+Animation}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Class} {\ttfamily add\+Init\+Hook} method for {\bfseries{adding constructor hooks to any classes}} (great extension point for plugin authors). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1123}{\texttt{\#1123}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily when\+Ready} method (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1063}{\texttt{\#1063}}
\item Added optional {\ttfamily delta} argument to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily zoom\+In} and {\ttfamily zoom\+Out} (1 by default).
\item Added {\ttfamily is\+Valid} method to {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} and {\ttfamily Bounds} (by \href{https://github.com/domoritz}{\texttt{@domoritz}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/972}{\texttt{\#972}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Point} {\ttfamily equals} method.
\item Added {\ttfamily Bounds} {\ttfamily get\+Size} method.
\item Improved markers and vectors click event so that it propagates to map if no one is listening to it (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/834}{\texttt{\#834}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1033}{\texttt{\#1033}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Path} {\ttfamily unbind\+Popup} and {\ttfamily close\+Popup} methods.
\item Added {\ttfamily Path} {\ttfamily add} and {\ttfamily remove} event.
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily rise\+On\+Hover} and {\ttfamily rise\+Offset} options (for bringing markers to front on hover, disabled by default) (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/914}{\texttt{\#914}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/920}{\texttt{\#920}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily move} and {\ttfamily remove} events.
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily contextmenu} event. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/223}{\texttt{\#223}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily zoom\+Animation} option (useful to disable when displaying flash content inside popups \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/999}{\texttt{\#999}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily layeradd} and {\ttfamily layerremove} events (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1122}{\texttt{\#1122}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} {\ttfamily baselayerchange} event (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1064}{\texttt{\#1064}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} to support HTML in layer names (by \href{https://github.com/aparshin}{\texttt{@aparshin}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1055}{\texttt{\#1055}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1099}{\texttt{\#1099}}
\item Added {\ttfamily CRS.\+Simple} to the list of built-\/in CRS and improved it to be more usable out of the box (it has different default scaling and transformation now), see {\ttfamily debug/\+map/\+simple-\/proj.\+html} for an example.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Browser} {\ttfamily ua}, {\ttfamily gecko}, {\ttfamily opera} properties (no longer needed).
\item Added {\ttfamily L.\+extend}, {\ttfamily L.\+bind}, {\ttfamily L.\+stamp}, {\ttfamily L.\+set\+Options} shortcuts for corresponding {\ttfamily L.\+Util} methods.
\item Disabled clearing of map container contents on map initialization (as a result of fixing \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/278}{\texttt{\#278}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily L.\+Util.\+is\+Array} function (by \href{https://github.com/oslek}{\texttt{@oslek}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1279}{\texttt{\#1279}}
\item Added {\ttfamily mouseover} and {\ttfamily mouseout} events to canvas-\/based vector layers (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1403}{\texttt{\#1403}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily each\+Layer} to iterate over all layers added to the map (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1457}{\texttt{\#1457}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily bounds} option to limit tile loading to a specific region (by \href{https://github.com/adimitrov}{\texttt{@adimitrov}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/991}{\texttt{\#991}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Bugfixes

\#\#\#\# General bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed broken tiles and zooming in RTL layouts (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1099}{\texttt{\#1099}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1095}{\texttt{\#1095}}
\item Fixed a bug with pan animation where it jumped to its end position if you tried to drag the map.
\item Fixed a bug where shift-\/clicking on a map would zoom it to the max zoom level.
\item Fixed a glitch with zooming in while panning animation is running.
\item Fixed a glitch with dragging the map while zoom animation is running.
\item Fixed a bug where slight touchpad scrolling or one-\/wheel scrolling wouln\textquotesingle{}t always perform zooming. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1039}{\texttt{\#1039}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily pan\+By} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t round the offset values (so it was possible to make the map blurry with it). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1085}{\texttt{\#1085}}
\item Fixed a bug where you couldn\textquotesingle{}t scroll the layers control with a mouse wheel.
\item Fixed a regression where WMS tiles wouldn\textquotesingle{}t wrap on date lines. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/970}{\texttt{\#970}}
\item Fixed a bug where mouse interaction was affected by map container border width (by \href{https://github.com/mohlendo}{\texttt{@mohlendo}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1205}{\texttt{\#1204}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1205}{\texttt{\#1205}}
\item Fixed a bug with weird vector zoom animation when using Canvas for rendering (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1187}{\texttt{\#1187}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1188}{\texttt{\#1188}}
\item Fixed a bug where max bounds limitation didn\textquotesingle{}t work when navigating the map with a keyboard (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/989}{\texttt{\#989}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1221}{\texttt{\#1221}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Back} didn\textquotesingle{}t work properly in some cases (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/963}{\texttt{\#963}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/959}{\texttt{\#959}}
\item Fixed a bug where removing a tile layer while dragging would throw an error (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/965}{\texttt{\#965}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/968}{\texttt{\#968}}
\item Fixed a bug where middle marker wasn\textquotesingle{}t removed after deleting 2 end nodes from a polyline (by \href{https://github.com/Svad}{\texttt{@Svad}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1022}{\texttt{\#1022}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1023}{\texttt{\#1023}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily load} event happened too late (after {\ttfamily moveend}, etc.) (by \href{https://github.com/jfirebaugh}{\texttt{@jfirebaugh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1027}{\texttt{\#1027}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Circle} {\ttfamily get\+Bounds} to return correct bounds and work without adding the circle to a map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1068}{\texttt{\#1068}}
\item Fixed a bug where removing {\ttfamily Popup} on {\ttfamily viewreset} throwed an error (by \href{https://github.com/fnicollet}{\texttt{fnicollet}} and \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1098}{\texttt{\#1098}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1094}{\texttt{\#1094}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+Canvas} {\ttfamily draw\+Tile} didn\textquotesingle{}t receive tile zoom level in arguments.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily reset\+Style} would not fully reset a layer to its default style. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1112}{\texttt{\#1112}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused infinite recursion when using {\ttfamily lat\+Lng\+Bounds} factory with coordinates as string values. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/933}{\texttt{\#933}}
\item Fixed chaining on {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Icon}, {\ttfamily set\+ZIndex\+Offset}, {\ttfamily update} methods. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1176}{\texttt{\#1176}}
\item Fixed a bug with mouse interaction when the map container contained children with position other than absolute. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/278}{\texttt{\#278}}
\item Fixed a bug with fill/\+stroke opacity conflicts when using Canvas for rendering (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1186}{\texttt{\#1186}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1189}{\texttt{\#1889}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily bind\+Popup} didn\textquotesingle{}t take options into account.
\item Fixed a bug where Canvas-\/based vector layers didn\textquotesingle{}t cleanup click event on removal properly (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1006}{\texttt{\#1006}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1273}{\texttt{\#1273}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Circle\+Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Style} didn\textquotesingle{}t take {\ttfamily radius} into account (by \href{https://github.com/fdlk}{\texttt{@fdlk}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1012}{\texttt{\#1012}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1013}{\texttt{\#1013}}
\item Fixed a bug where null Geo\+JSON geometries would throw an error instead of skipping (by \href{https://github.com/brianherbert}{\texttt{@brianherbert}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1240}{\texttt{\#1240}}
\item Fixed a bug where Canvas-\/based vector layers passed incorrect {\ttfamily layer} event property on click (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1215}{\texttt{\#1215}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1243}{\texttt{\#1243}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} didn\textquotesingle{}t work correctly if the base URL contained query parameters (by \href{https://github.com/snkashis}{\texttt{@snkashis}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/973}{\texttt{\#973}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1231}{\texttt{\#1231}}
\item Fixed a bug where removing a polyline in editing state wouldn\textquotesingle{}t clean up the editing handles (by \href{https://github.com/mehmeta}{\texttt{@mehmeta}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1233}{\texttt{\#1233}}
\item Fixed a bug where removing a vector layer with a bound popup wouldn\textquotesingle{}t clean up its click event properly (by \href{https://github.com/yohanboniface}{\texttt{@yohanboniface}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1229}{\texttt{\#1229}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} features with {\ttfamily Geometry\+Collection} didn\textquotesingle{}t pass properties to {\ttfamily point\+To\+Layer} function (by \href{https://github.com/calvinmetcalf}{\texttt{@calvinmetcalf}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1097}{\texttt{\#1097}}
\item Fixed {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily each\+Layer} chaining. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1452}{\texttt{\#1452}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug with map {\bfseries{freezing after zoom on Android 4.\+1}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1182}{\texttt{\#1182}}
\item Fixed a bug where "{}\+Not implemented"{} error sometimes appeared in IE6-\/8 (by \href{https://github.com/bryguy}{\texttt{@bryguy}} and \href{https://github.com/lookfirst}{\texttt{@lookfirst}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/892}{\texttt{\#892}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/893}{\texttt{\#893}}
\item Fixed compatibility with Smooth\+Wheel extension for Firefox (by \href{https://github.com/waldir}{\texttt{@waldir}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1011}{\texttt{\#1011}}
\item Fixed a bug with popup layout in IE6-\/7 (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1117}{\texttt{\#1117}}
\item Fixed a bug with incorrect box zoom opacity in IE6-\/7 (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://githubcom/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1072}{\texttt{\#1072}}
\item Fixed a bug with box zoom throwing a JS error in IE6-\/7 (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1071}{\texttt{\#1071}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Front/\+\+Back()} throwed an error in IE6-\/8. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1168}{\texttt{\#1168}}
\item Fixed array type checking in the code to be more consistent in a cross-\/frame environment (by \href{https://github.com/oslek}{\texttt{@oslek}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1279}{\texttt{\#1279}}
\item Fixed a bug with {\ttfamily -\/} key not working in Firefox 15+ (thanks to \href{https://github.com/mattesCZ}{\texttt{@mattes\+CZ}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/869}{\texttt{\#869}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+4.\+5 (2012-\/10-\/25)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug with {\bfseries{wonky zoom animation in IE10}} (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1007}{\texttt{\#1007}}
\item Fixed a bug with {\bfseries{wonky zoom animation in Chrome 23+}} (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/1060}{\texttt{\#1060}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/1056}{\texttt{\#1056}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+4.\+4 (2012-\/08-\/07)

\#\#\# Improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily set\+Style} to also accept function (like the corresponding option).
\item Added {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily reset\+Style(layer)}, useful for resetting hover state.
\item Added {\ttfamily feature} property to layers created with {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} (containing the Geo\+JSON feature data).
\item Added {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Front} and {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Back} methods (so that they would work for multipolys).
\item Added optional {\ttfamily animate} argument to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily invalidate\+Size} (by \href{https://github.com/ajbeaven}{\texttt{@ajbeaven}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/857}{\texttt{\#857}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where tiles sometimes disappeared on initial map load on Android 2/\+3 (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/868}{\texttt{\#868}}
\item Fixed a bug where map would occasionally flicker near the border on zoom or pan on Chrome.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Path} {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Front} and {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Back} didn\textquotesingle{}t return {\ttfamily this}.
\item Removed zoom out on Win/\+\+Meta key binding (since it interferes with global keyboard shortcuts). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/869}{\texttt{\#869}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+4.\+2 (2012-\/08-\/01)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where layers control radio buttons would not work correctly in IE7 (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/862}{\texttt{\#862}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily remove\+Layer} would unbind popups of removed layers even if the popups were not put by the group (affected \href{https://github.com/danzel/Leaflet.markercluster}{\texttt{Leaflet.\+markercluster}} plugin) (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/861}{\texttt{\#861}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+4.\+1 (2012-\/07-\/31)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that caused marker shadows appear as opaque black in IE6-\/8. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/850}{\texttt{\#850}}
\item Fixed a bug with incorrect calculation of scale by the scale control. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/852}{\texttt{\#852}}
\item Fixed broken L.\+tile\+Layer.\+wms class factory (by \href{https://github.com/mattcurrie}{\texttt{@mattcurrie}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/856}{\texttt{\#856}}
\item Improved retina detection for {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily detect\+Retina} option (by \href{https://github.com/sxua}{\texttt{@sxua}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/854}{\texttt{\#854}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+4 (2012-\/07-\/30)

\#\#\# API simplification

Leaflet 0.\+4 contains several API improvements that allow simpler, j\+Query-\/like syntax (\href{https://gist.github.com/3038879}{\texttt{example}}) while being backwards compatible with the previous approach (so you can use both styles):\+


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved most methods and options to accept {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng}, {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds}, {\ttfamily Point} and {\ttfamily Bounds} values in an array form (e.\+g. {\ttfamily map.\+pan\+To(\+[lat, lng]\+)} will be the same as {\ttfamily map.\+pan\+To(new L.\+Lat\+Lng(lat, lng))})
\item Added {\ttfamily add\+To} method to all layer classes, e.\+g. {\ttfamily marker.\+add\+To(map)} is equivalent to {\ttfamily map.\+add\+Layer(marker)}
\item Added factory methods to most classes to be able to write code without {\ttfamily new} keyword, named the same as classes but starting with a lowercase letter, e.\+g. {\ttfamily L.\+map(\textquotesingle{}map\textquotesingle{})} is the same as {\ttfamily new L.\+Map(\textquotesingle{}map\textquotesingle{})}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Notable new features


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added configurable {\bfseries{panning inertia}} -\/ after a quick pan, the map slows down in the same direction.
\item Added {\bfseries{keyboard navigation}} for panning/\+zooming with keyboard arrows and +/\+-\/ keys (by \href{https://github.com/ericmmartinez}{\texttt{@ericmmartinez}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/663}{\texttt{\#663}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/646}{\texttt{\#646}}
\item Added smooth {\bfseries{zoom animation of markers, vector layers, image overlays and popups}} (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/740}{\texttt{\#740}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/758}{\texttt{\#758}}
\item Added {\bfseries{Android 4+ pinch-\/zoom}} support (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/774}{\texttt{\#774}}
\item Added {\bfseries{polyline and polygon editing}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/174}{\texttt{\#174}}
\item Added an unobtrusive {\bfseries{scale control}}.
\item Added {\bfseries{Div\+Icon}} class that easily allows you to create lightweight div-\/based markers.
\item Added {\bfseries{Rectangle}} vector layer (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/504}{\texttt{\#504}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Improvements

\#\#\#\# Usability improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved zooming so that you don\textquotesingle{}t get a blank map when you zoom in or out twice quickly (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/7}{\texttt{\#7}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/729}{\texttt{\#729}}
\item Drag-\/panning now works even when there are markers in the starting point (helps on maps with lots of markers). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/506}{\texttt{\#506}}
\item Improved panning performance even more (there are no wasted frames now).
\item Improved pinch-\/zoom performance in mobile Chrome and Firefox.
\item Improved map performance on window resize.
\item Replaced box-\/shadow with border on controls for mobile devices to improve performance.
\item Slightly improved default popup styling.
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily detect\+Retina} option ({\ttfamily false} by default) that makes tiles show in a higher resolution on i\+OS retina displays (by \href{https://github.com/Mithgol}{\texttt{@Mithgol}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/586}{\texttt{\#586}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Geo\+JSON API changes

Geo\+JSON API was improved to be simpler and more flexible (\href{https://gist.github.com/3062900}{\texttt{example}}). The changes are not backwards-\/compatible, so be sure to update your old code.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily style} option for styling vector layers, passed either as an object or as a function (to style vector layers according to Geo\+JSON properties).
\item Added {\ttfamily filter} option to leave out features that don\textquotesingle{}t correspond to a certain criteria (e.\+g. based on properties).
\item Added {\ttfamily on\+Each\+Feature} option to execute certain code on each feature layer based on its properties (binding popups, etc).
\item Changed {\ttfamily point\+To\+Layer} function signature to provide {\ttfamily geojson} in addition to {\ttfamily latlng} when creating point features for more flexibility.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Icon API changes

Icon API was improved to be more flexible, but one of the changes is backwards-\/incompatible:\+ you now need to pass different icon properties (like {\ttfamily icon\+Url}) inside an options object (\href{https://gist.github.com/3076084}{\texttt{example}}).


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Converted {\ttfamily Icon} properties to options, changed constructor signature to {\ttfamily Icon(options)}.
\item Moved default marker icon options to {\ttfamily L.\+Icon.\+Default} class (which extends from {\ttfamily L.\+Icon}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Icon} {\ttfamily class\+Name} option to assign a custom class to an icon.
\item Added {\ttfamily Icon} {\ttfamily shadow\+Anchor} option to set the anchor of the shadow.
\item Made all {\ttfamily Icon} options except {\ttfamily icon\+Url} optional (if not specified, they\textquotesingle{}ll be chosen automatically or implemented using CSS). Anchor is centered by default (if size is specified), and otherwise can be set through CSS using negative margins.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Control API changes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+Position} and {\ttfamily get\+Position} to all controls, as well as ability to pass certain position as an option when creating a control.
\item Made controls implementation easier (now more magic happens under the hood).
\item Replaced ugly control position constants (e.\+g. {\ttfamily L.\+Control.\+Position.\+TOP\+\_\+\+LEFT}) with light strings ({\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}topleft\textquotesingle{}}, {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}bottomright\textquotesingle{}}, etc.)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Other breaking API changes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} constructor to interpolate URL template values from options (removed third {\ttfamily url\+Params} argument).
\item Changed {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily scheme:\+ \textquotesingle{}tms\textquotesingle{}} option to {\ttfamily tms:\+ true}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily locate\+And\+Set\+View} method (use {\ttfamily locate} with {\ttfamily set\+View:\+ true} option)
\item Changed popup {\ttfamily min\+Width} and {\ttfamily max\+Width} options to be applied to content element, not the whole popup.
\item Moved {\ttfamily prefix} argument to {\ttfamily options} in {\ttfamily Control.\+Attribution} constructor.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily L.\+VERSION} to {\ttfamily L.\+version}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Other API improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved {\ttfamily on} and {\ttfamily off} methods to also accept {\ttfamily (event\+Hash\+[, context]\+)}, as well as multiple space-\/separated events (by \href{https://github.com/Guiswa}{\texttt{@Guiswa}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/770}{\texttt{\#770}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily off} to remove all listeners of the event if no function was specified (by \href{https://github.com/Guiswa}{\texttt{@Guiswa}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/770}{\texttt{\#770}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/691}{\texttt{\#691}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily set\+ZIndex} method for controlling the order of tile layers (thanks to \href{https://github.com/mattcurrie}{\texttt{@mattcurrie}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/837}{\texttt{\#837}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} {\ttfamily auto\+ZIndex} option (on by default) to preserve the order of tile layers when switching.
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily redraw} method for re-\/requesting tiles (by \href{https://github.com/greeninfo}{\texttt{@greeninfo}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/719}{\texttt{\#719}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily set\+Url} method for dynamically changing the tile URL template.
\item Added {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Front} and {\ttfamily bring\+To\+Back} methods to {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer}, {\ttfamily Image\+Overlay} and vector layers. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/185}{\texttt{\#185}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/505}{\texttt{\#505}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily loading} event that fires when its tiles start to load (thanks to \href{https://github.com/lapinos03}{\texttt{@lapinos03}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/177}{\texttt{\#177}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} {\ttfamily set\+Params} method for setting WMS parameters at runtime (by \href{https://github.com/greeninfo}{\texttt{@greeninfo}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/719}{\texttt{\#719}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} subdomain support ({\ttfamily \{s\}} in the url) (by \href{https://github.com/greeninfo}{\texttt{@greeninfo}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/735}{\texttt{\#735}}
\item Added {\ttfamily original\+Event} property to {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event} (by \href{https://github.com/k4}{\texttt{@k4}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/521}{\texttt{\#521}}
\item Added {\ttfamily container\+Point} property to {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/413}{\texttt{\#413}}
\item Added {\ttfamily contextmenu} event to vector layers (by \href{https://github.com/ErrorProne}{\texttt{@Error\+Prone}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/500}{\texttt{\#500}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily each\+Layer} method for iterating over its members.
\item Added {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily mousemove} and {\ttfamily contextmenu} events (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/816}{\texttt{\#816}}
\item Added chaining to {\ttfamily Dom\+Event} methods.
\item Added {\ttfamily on} and {\ttfamily off} aliases for {\ttfamily Dom\+Event} {\ttfamily add\+Listener} and {\ttfamily remove\+Listener} methods.
\item Added {\ttfamily L\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+TOUCH} global variable switch (set it before Leaflet inclusion) which disables touch detection, helpful for desktop apps built using QT. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/572}{\texttt{\#572}}
\item Added {\ttfamily dash\+Array} option to vector layers for making dashed strokes (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/821}{\texttt{\#821}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/165}{\texttt{\#165}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Circle} {\ttfamily get\+Bounds} method. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/440}{\texttt{\#440}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Circle} {\ttfamily get\+Lat\+Lng} and {\ttfamily get\+Radius} methods (by \href{https://github.com/Guiswa}{\texttt{@Guiswa}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/655}{\texttt{\#655}}
\item Added {\ttfamily open\+Popup} method to all vector layers. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/246}{\texttt{\#246}}
\item Added public {\ttfamily redraw} method to vector layers (useful if you manipulate their {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} points directly).
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily opacity} option and {\ttfamily set\+Opacity} method.
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily update} method. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/392}{\texttt{\#392}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily open\+Popup} not to raise an error if it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a popup. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/507}{\texttt{\#507}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Image\+Overlay} {\ttfamily opacity} option and {\ttfamily set\+Opacity} method. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/438}{\texttt{\#438}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily max\+Height} option that makes content inside the popup scrolled if it doesn\textquotesingle{}t fit the specified max height.
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily open\+On(map)} method (similar to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily open\+Popup}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily get\+Container} method (by \href{https://github.com/Guiswa}{\texttt{@Guiswa}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/654}{\texttt{\#654}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily container\+Point\+To\+Lat\+Lng} and {\ttfamily lat\+Lng\+To\+Container\+Point} methods. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/474}{\texttt{\#474}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily add\+Handler} method.
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily mouseup} and {\ttfamily autopanstart} events.
\item Added {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily pad} method that returns bounds extended by a percentage (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/492}{\texttt{\#492}}
\item Moved dragging cursor styles from JS code to CSS.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Bug fixes

\#\#\#\# General bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where the map was zooming incorrectly inside a {\ttfamily position:\+ fixed} container (by \href{https://github.com/chx007}{\texttt{@chx007}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/602}{\texttt{\#602}}
\item Fixed a bug where scaled tiles weren\textquotesingle{}t cleared up after zoom in some cases (by \href{https://github.com/cfis}{\texttt{@cfis}}) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/683}{\texttt{\#683}}
\item Fixed a bug where map wouldn\textquotesingle{}t drag over a polygon with a {\ttfamily mousedown} listener. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/834}{\texttt{\#834}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression where remove\+Layer would not remove corresponding attribution. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/488}{\texttt{\#488}}
\item Fixed a bug where popup close button wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work on manually added popups. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/423}{\texttt{\#423}}
\item Fixed a bug where marker click event would stop working if you dragged it and then disabled dragging. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/434}{\texttt{\#434}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily set\+Opacity} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work when setting it back to 1.
\item Fixed a bug where vector layer {\ttfamily set\+Style(\{stroke:\+ false\})} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t remove stroke and the same for fill. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/441}{\texttt{\#441}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily bind\+Popup} method wouldn\textquotesingle{}t take {\ttfamily offset} option into account.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily load} event wasn\textquotesingle{}t fired if some tile didn\textquotesingle{}t load (by \href{https://github.com/lapinos03}{\texttt{@lapinos03}} and \href{https://github.com/cfis}{\texttt{@cfis}}) \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/682}{\texttt{\#682}}
\item Fixed error when removing {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} layer. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/685}{\texttt{\#685}}
\item Fixed error when calling {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily clear\+Layer} (by \href{https://github.com/runderwood}{\texttt{@runderwood}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/617}{\texttt{\#617}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Control} {\ttfamily set\+Position} wasn\textquotesingle{}t always working correctly (by \href{https://github.com/ericmmartinez}{\texttt{@ericmmartinez}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/657}{\texttt{\#657}}
\item Fixed a bug with {\ttfamily Util.\+bind} sometimes losing arguments (by \href{https://github.com/johtso}{\texttt{@johtso}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/588}{\texttt{\#588}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily drag} event was sometimes fired after {\ttfamily dragend}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/555}{\texttt{\#555}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily load} event was firing only once (by \href{https://github.com/lapinos03}{\texttt{@lapinos03}} and \href{https://github.com/shintonik}{\texttt{shintonik}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/742}{\texttt{\#742}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/177}{\texttt{\#177}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} popup events where not cleaned up after removing a layer from it (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/775}{\texttt{\#775}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Dom\+Util.\+remove\+Class} didn\textquotesingle{}t remove trailing spaces (by \href{https://github.com/jieter}{\texttt{@jieter}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/784}{\texttt{\#784}}
\item Fixed a bug where marker popup didn\textquotesingle{}t take popup offset into account.
\item Fixed a bug that led to an error when polyline was removed inside a {\ttfamily moveend} listener.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Layer\+Group} {\ttfamily add\+Layer} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t check if a layer has already been added (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/798}{\texttt{798}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed broken zooming on IE10 beta (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/650}{\texttt{\#650}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/751}{\texttt{\#751}}
\item Fixed a bug that broke Leaflet for websites that had XHTML content-\/type header set (by \href{https://github.com/lars-sh}{\texttt{lars-\/sh}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/801}{\texttt{\#801}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused popups to be empty in IE when passing a DOM node as the content (by \href{https://github.com/nrenner}{\texttt{@nrenner}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/472}{\texttt{\#472}}
\item Fixed inability to use scrolled content inside popup due to mouse wheel propagation.
\item Fixed a bug that caused jumping/\+stuttering of panning animation in some cases.
\item Fixed a bug where popup size was calculated incorrectly in IE.
\item Fixed a bug where cursor would flicker when dragging a marker.
\item Fixed a bug where clickable paths on IE9 didn\textquotesingle{}t have a hand cursor (by \href{https://github.com/naehrstoff}{\texttt{naehrstoff}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/671}{\texttt{\#671}}
\item Fixed a bug in IE with disappearing icons when changing opacity (by \href{https://github.com/tagliala}{\texttt{@tagliala}} and \href{https://github.com/DamonOehlman}{\texttt{Damon\+Oehlman}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/667}{\texttt{\#667}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/600}{\texttt{\#600}}
\item Fixed a bug with setting opacity on IE10 (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/796}{\texttt{796}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Control.\+Layers} didn\textquotesingle{}t work on IE7. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/652}{\texttt{\#652}}
\item Fixed a bug that could cause false {\ttfamily mousemove} events on click in Chrome (by \href{https://github.com/stsydow}{\texttt{@stsydow}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/757}{\texttt{\#757}}
\item Fixed a bug in IE6-\/8 where adding fill or stroke on vector layers after initialization with {\ttfamily set\+Style} would break the map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/641}{\texttt{\#641}}
\item Fixed a bug with set\+Opacity in IE where it would not work correctly if used more than once on the same element (by \href{https://github.com/ajbeaven}{\texttt{@ajbeaven}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/827}{\texttt{\#827}}
\item Fixed a bug in Chrome where transparent control corners sometimes couldn\textquotesingle{}t be clicked through (by \href{https://github.com/danzel}{\texttt{@danzel}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/836}{\texttt{\#836}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/575}{\texttt{\#575}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Mobile browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that sometimes caused map to disappear completely after zoom on i\+OS (by \href{https://github.com/fr1n63}{\texttt{@fr1n63}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/580}{\texttt{\#580}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/777}{\texttt{\#777}}
\item Fixed a bug that often caused vector layers to flicker on drag end on i\+OS (by \href{https://github.com/krawaller}{\texttt{@krawaller}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/18}{\texttt{\#18}}
\item Fixed a bug with false map click events on pinch-\/zoom and zoom/\+layers controls click. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/485}{\texttt{\#485}}
\item Fixed a bug where touching the map with two or more fingers simultaneously would raise an error.
\item Fixed a bug where zoom control wasn\textquotesingle{}t always visible on Android 3. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/335}{\texttt{\#335}}
\item Fixed a bug where opening the layers control would propagate a click to the map (by \href{https://github.com/jacobtoye}{\texttt{@jacobtoye}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/638}{\texttt{\#638}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Image\+Overlay} wouldn\textquotesingle{}t stretch properly on zoom on Android 2. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/651}{\texttt{\#651}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily clear\+Layers} for vector layers on a Canvas backend (e.\+g. on Android 2) would take unreasonable amount of time. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/785}{\texttt{\#785}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lngs} and similar methods on vector layers on a Canvas backend would not update the layers immediately. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/732}{\texttt{\#732}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+3.\+1 (2012-\/02-\/14)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression where default marker icons wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work if Leaflet include url contained a query string.
