\item Fixed a regression where tiles sometimes flickered with black on panning in i\+OS.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+3 (2012-\/02-\/13)

\#\#\# Major features


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{Canvas backend}} for vector layers (polylines, polygons, circles). This enables vector support on Android \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 3, and it can also be optionally preferred over SVG for a performance gain in some cases. Thanks to \href{https://github.com/florianf}{\texttt{@florianf}} for a big part of this work.
\item Added {\bfseries{layers control}} ({\ttfamily Control.\+Layers}) for convenient layer switching.
\item Added ability to set {\bfseries{max bounds}} within which users can pan/\+zoom. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/93}{\texttt{\#93}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Improvements

\#\#\#\# Usability improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Map now preserves its center after resize.
\item When panning to another copy of the world (that\textquotesingle{}s infinite horizontally), map overlays now jump to corresponding positions. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/273}{\texttt{\#273}}
\item Limited maximum zoom change on a single mouse wheel movement (so you won\textquotesingle{}t zoom across the whole zoom range in one scroll). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/149}{\texttt{\#149}}
\item Significantly improved line simplification performance (noticeable when rendering polylines/\+polygons with tens of thousands of points)
\item Improved circles performance by not drawing them if they\textquotesingle{}re off the clip region.
\item Improved stability of zoom animation (less flickering of tiles).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added ability to add a tile layer below all others ({\ttfamily map.\+add\+Layer(layer, true)}) (useful for switching base tile layers).
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily zoomstart} event (thanks to \href{https://github.com/Fabiz}{\texttt{@Fabiz}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/377}{\texttt{\#377}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily locate} method, added ability to watch location continuously and more options. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/212}{\texttt{\#212}}
\item Added second argument {\ttfamily inside} to {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily get\+Bounds\+Zoom} method that allows you to get appropriate zoom for the view to fit {\itshape inside} the given bounds.
\item Added {\ttfamily has\+Layer} method to {\ttfamily Map}.
\item Added {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily z\+Index\+Offset} option to be able to set certain markers below/\+above others. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/65}{\texttt{\#65}}
\item Added {\ttfamily url\+Params} third optional argument to {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} constructor for convenience:\+ an object with properties that will be evaluated in the URL template.
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily continuous\+World} option to disable tile coordinates checking/\+wrapping.
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily tileunload} event fired when tile gets removed after panning (by \href{https://github.com/CodeJosch}{\texttt{@Code\+Josch}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/256}{\texttt{\#256}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily zoom\+Offset} option useful for non-\/256px tiles (by \href{https://github.com/msaspence}{\texttt{@msaspence}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily zoom\+Reverse} option to reverse zoom numbering (by \href{https://github.com/Majiir}{\texttt{@Majiir}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/406}{\texttt{\#406}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+Canvas} {\ttfamily redraw} method (by \href{https://github.com/mortenbekditlevsen}{\texttt{@mortenbekditlevsen}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/459}{\texttt{\#459}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Polyline} {\ttfamily closest\+Layer\+Point} method that\textquotesingle{}s can be useful for interaction features (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/186}{\texttt{\#186}}
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lngs} method to {\ttfamily Multi\+Polyline} and {\ttfamily Multi\+Polygon} (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/194}{\texttt{\#194}}
\item Added {\ttfamily get\+Bounds} method to {\ttfamily Polyline} and {\ttfamily Polygon} (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/253}{\texttt{\#253}}
\item Added {\ttfamily get\+Bounds} method to {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/557}{\texttt{\#557}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily set\+Style} method (also inherited by {\ttfamily Multi\+Polyline} and {\ttfamily Multi\+Polygon}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/353}{\texttt{\#353}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Feature\+Group} {\ttfamily invoke} method to call a particular method on all layers of the group with the given arguments.
\item Added {\ttfamily Image\+Overlay} {\ttfamily load} event. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/213}{\texttt{\#213}}
\item Added {\ttfamily min\+Width} option to {\ttfamily Popup} (by \href{https://github.com/marphi}{\texttt{@marphi}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/214}{\texttt{\#214}}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} constructor to be more tolerant (and throw descriptive error if latitude or longitude can\textquotesingle{}t be interpreted as a number). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/136}{\texttt{\#136}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} {\ttfamily distance\+To} method (great circle distance) (by \href{https://github.com/mortenbekditlevsen}{\texttt{@mortenbekditlevsen}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/462}{\texttt{\#462}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily to\+BBox\+String} method for convenience (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/263}{\texttt{\#263}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily intersects(other\+Bounds)} method (thanks to \href{https://github.com/pagameba}{\texttt{@pagameba}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/350}{\texttt{\#350}}
\item Made {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} {\ttfamily extend} method to accept other {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} in addition to {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/553}{\texttt{\#553}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Bounds} {\ttfamily intersects(other\+Bounds)} method. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/461}{\texttt{\#461}}
\item Added {\ttfamily L.\+Util.\+template} method for simple string template evaluation.
\item Added {\ttfamily Dom\+Util.\+remove\+Class} method (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}).
\item Improved browser-\/specific code to rely more on feature detection rather than user agent string.
\item Improved superclass access mechanism to work with inheritance chains of 3 or more classes; now you should use {\ttfamily Klass.\+superclass} instead of {\ttfamily this.\+superclass} (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/179}{\texttt{\#179}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily boxzoomstart} and {\ttfamily boxzoomend} events (by \href{https://github.com/zedd45}{\texttt{@zedd45}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/554}{\texttt{\#554}}
\item Added {\ttfamily Popup} {\ttfamily contentupdate} event (by \href{https://github.com/mehmeta}{\texttt{@mehmeta}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/548}{\texttt{\#548}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Breaking API changes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily shift\+Drag\+Zoom} map option/\+property renamed to {\ttfamily box\+Zoom}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily mouse\+Event\+To\+Lat\+Lng} method (bringed back in 0.\+4).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Development workflow improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Build system completely overhauled to be based on Node.\+js, Jake, JSHint and Uglify\+JS.
\item All code is now linted for errors and conformity with a strict code style (with JSHint), and wont build unless the check passes.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Bugfixes

\#\#\#\# General bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Circle} was rendered with incorrect radius (didn\textquotesingle{}t take projection exagerration into account). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/331}{\texttt{\#331}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Map} {\ttfamily get\+Bounds} would work incorrectly on a date line cross. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/295}{\texttt{\#295}}
\item Fixed a bug where polygons and polylines sometimes rendered incorrectly on some zoom levels. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/381}{\texttt{\#381}}
\item Fixed a bug where fast mouse wheel zoom worked incorrectly when approaching min/\+max zoom values.
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Geo\+JSON} {\ttfamily point\+To\+Layer} option wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work in a {\ttfamily Geometry\+Collection}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/391}{\texttt{\#391}}
\item Fixed a bug with incorrect rendering of Geo\+JSON on a date line cross. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/354}{\texttt{\#354}}
\item Fixed a bug where map panning would stuck forever after releasing the mouse over an iframe or a flash object (thanks to \href{https://github.com/sten82}{\texttt{@sten82}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/297}{\texttt{\#297}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/64}{\texttt{\#64}}
\item Fixed a bug where mouse wheel zoom worked incorrectly if map is inside scrolled container (partially by \href{https://github.com/chrillo}{\texttt{@chrillo}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/206}{\texttt{\#206}}
\item Fixed a bug where it was possible to add the same listener twice. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/281}{\texttt{\#281}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Circle} was rendered with incorrect radius (didn\textquotesingle{}t take projection exaggeration into account). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/331}{\texttt{\#331}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Icon} was not working properly (by \href{https://github.com/marphi}{\texttt{@marphi}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/218}{\texttt{\#218}} \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/311}{\texttt{\#311}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lng} was not working if it\textquotesingle{}s set before adding the marker to a map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/222}{\texttt{\#222}}
\item Fixed a bug where marker popup would not move on {\ttfamily Marker} {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lng} (by \href{https://github.com/tjarratt}{\texttt{@tjarratt}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/272}{\texttt{\#272}}
\item Fixed a bug where static properties of a child class would not override the parent ones.
\item Fixed broken popup {\ttfamily close\+Popup} option (by \href{https://github.com/jgerigmeyer}{\texttt{@jgerigmeyer}}).
\item Fixed a bug that caused en error when dragging marker with icon without shadow (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/178}{\texttt{\#178}}
\item Fixed a typo in {\ttfamily Bounds} {\ttfamily contains} method (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/180}{\texttt{\#180}}
\item Fixed a bug where creating an empty {\ttfamily Polygon} with {\ttfamily new L.\+Polygon()} would raise an error.
\item Fixed a bug where drag event fired before the actual movement of layer (by \href{https://github.com/anru}{\texttt{@anru}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/197}{\texttt{\#197}}
\item Fixed a bug where map click caused an error if dragging is initially disabled. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/196}{\texttt{\#196}}
\item Fixed a bug where map {\ttfamily movestart} event would fire after zoom animation.
\item Fixed a bug where attribution prefix would not update on {\ttfamily set\+Prefix}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/195}{\texttt{\#195}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily load} event wouldn\textquotesingle{}t fire in some edge cases (by \href{https://github.com/dravnic}{\texttt{@dravnic}}).
\item Fixed a bug related to clearing background tiles after zooming (by \href{https://github.com/neno-giscloud}{\texttt{@neno-\/giscloud}} \& \href{https://github.com/dravnic}{\texttt{@dravnic}}).
\item Fixed a bug that sometimes caused map flickering after zoom animation.
\item Fixed a bug related to cleaning up after removing tile layers (by \href{https://github.com/dravnic}{\texttt{@dravnic}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/276}{\texttt{\#276}}
\item Fixed a bug that made selecting text in the attribution control impossible. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/279}{\texttt{\#279}}
\item Fixed a bug when initializing a map in a non-\/empty div. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/278}{\texttt{\#278}}
\item Fixed a bug where {\ttfamily movestart} didn\textquotesingle{}t fire on panning animation.
\item Fixed a bug in Elliptical Mercator formula that affeted {\ttfamily EPSG:\+3395} CRS (by \href{https://github.com/Savvkin}{\texttt{@Savvkin}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/358}{\texttt{\#358}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed occasional crashes on Mac Safari (thanks to \href{https://github.com/lapinos03}{\texttt{@lapinos03}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/191}{\texttt{\#191}}
\item Fixed a bug where resizing the map would sometimes make it blurry on Web\+Kit (by \href{https://github.com/mortenbekditlevsen}{\texttt{@mortenbekditlevsen}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/pull/453}{\texttt{\#453}}
\item Fixed a bug that raised error in IE6-\/8 when clicking on popup close button. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/235}{\texttt{\#235}}
\item Fixed a bug with Safari not redrawing UI immediately after closing a popup. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/296}{\texttt{\#296}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused performance drop and high CPU usage when calling {\ttfamily set\+View} or {\ttfamily pan\+To} to the current center. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/231}{\texttt{\#231}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused map overlays to appear blurry in some cases under Web\+Kit browsers.
\item Fixed a bug that was causing errors in some Webkit/\+\+Linux builds (request\+Animation\+Frame-\/related), thanks to Chris Martens.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Mobile browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that caused an error when clicking vector layers under i\+OS. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/204}{\texttt{\#204}}
\item Fixed crash on Android 3+ when panning or zooming (by \href{https://github.com/florianf}{\texttt{@florian}}). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/137}{\texttt{\#137}}
\item Fixed a bug on Android 2/\+3 that sometimes caused the map to disappear after zooming. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/69}{\texttt{\#69}}
\item Fixed a bug on Android 3 that caused tiles to shift position on a big map.
\item Fixed a bug that caused the map to pan when touch-\/panning inside a popup. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/452}{\texttt{\#452}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused click delays on zoom control.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+2.\+1 (2011-\/06-\/18)


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed regression that caused error in {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+Canvas}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+2 (2011-\/06-\/17)

\#\#\# Major features


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{WMS}} support ({\ttfamily Tile\+Layer.\+WMS} layer).
\item Added different {\bfseries{projections}} support, having {\ttfamily EPSG:\+3857}, {\ttfamily EPSG:\+4326} and {\ttfamily EPSG:\+3395} out of the box (through {\ttfamily crs} option in {\ttfamily Map}). Thanks to \href{https://github.com/Miroff}{\texttt{@Miroff}} \& \href{https://github.com/Komzpa}{\texttt{@Komzpa}} for great advice and explanation regarding this.
\item Added {\bfseries{Geo\+JSON}} layer support.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Improvements

\#\#\#\# Usability improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Improved panning performance in Chrome and FF considerably with the help of {\ttfamily request\+Animation\+Frame}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/130}{\texttt{\#130}}
\item Improved click responsiveness in mobile Web\+Kit (now it happens without delay). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/26}{\texttt{\#26}}
\item Added tap tolerance (so click happens even if you moved your finger slighly when tapping).
\item Improved geolocation error handling:\+ better error messages, explicit timeout, set world view on locate\+And\+Set\+View failure. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/61}{\texttt{\#61}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# API improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\bfseries{Multi\+Polyline}} and {\bfseries{Multi\+Polygon}} layers. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/77}{\texttt{\#77}}
\item Added {\bfseries{Layer\+Group}} and {\bfseries{Feature\+Group}} layers for grouping other layers.
\item Added {\bfseries{Tile\+Layer.\+Canvas}} for easy creation of canvas-\/based tile layers.
\item Changed {\ttfamily Circle} to be zoom-\/dependent (with radius in meters); circle of a permanent size is now called {\ttfamily Circle\+Marker}.
\item Added {\ttfamily mouseover} and {\ttfamily mouseout} events to map, markers and paths; added map {\ttfamily mousemove} event.
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lngs}, {\ttfamily splice\+Lat\+Lngs}, {\ttfamily add\+Lat\+Lng}, {\ttfamily get\+Lat\+Lngs} methods to polylines and polygons.
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lng} and {\ttfamily set\+Radius} methods to {\ttfamily Circle} and {\ttfamily Circle\+Marker}.
\item Improved {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds contains} method to accept {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng} in addition to {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds}, the same for {\ttfamily Bounds contains} and {\ttfamily Point}
\item Improved {\ttfamily Lat\+Lng\+Bounds} \& {\ttfamily Bounds} to allow their instantiation without arguments (by \href{https://github.com/snc}{\texttt{@snc}}).
\item Added TMS tile numbering support through {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily scheme:\+ \textquotesingle{}tms\textquotesingle{}} option (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer} {\ttfamily no\+Wrap} option to disable wrapping {\ttfamily x} tile coordinate (by \href{https://github.com/jasondavies}{\texttt{@jasondavies}}).
\item Added {\ttfamily opacity} option and {\ttfamily set\+Opacity} method to {\ttfamily Tile\+Layer}.
\item Added {\ttfamily set\+Lat\+Lng} and {\ttfamily set\+Icon} methods to {\ttfamily Marker}.
\item Added {\ttfamily title} option to {\ttfamily Marker}.
\item Added {\ttfamily max\+Zoom} argument to {\ttfamily map.\+locate\+And\+Set\+View} method.
\item Added ability to pass Geolocation options to map {\ttfamily locate} and {\ttfamily locate\+And\+Set\+View} methods (by \href{https://github.com/JasonSanford}{\texttt{@Jason\+Sanford}}).
\item Improved {\ttfamily Popup} to accept HTML elements in addition to strings as its content.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Development workflow improvements


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added {\ttfamily Makefile} for building {\ttfamily leaflet.\+js} on non-\/\+Windows machines (by \href{https://github.com/tmcw}{\texttt{@tmcw}}).
\item Improved {\ttfamily debug/\+leaflet-\/include.\+js} script to allow using it outside of {\ttfamily debug} folder (by \href{https://github.com/antonj}{\texttt{@antonj}}).
\item Improved {\ttfamily L} definition to be compatible with Common\+JS. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/122}{\texttt{\#122}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\# Bug fixes

\#\#\#\# General bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where zooming is broken if the map contains a polygon and you zoom to an area where it\textquotesingle{}s not visible. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/47}{\texttt{\#47}}
\item Fixed a bug where closed polylines would not appear on the map.
\item Fixed a bug where marker that was added, removed and then added again would not appear on the map. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/66}{\texttt{\#66}}
\item Fixed a bug where tile layer that was added, removed and then added again would not appear on the map.
\item Fixed a bug where some tiles would not load when panning across the date line. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/97}{\texttt{\#97}}
\item Fixed a bug where map div with {\ttfamily position:\+ absolute} is reset to {\ttfamily relative}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/100}{\texttt{\#100}}
\item Fixed a bug that caused an error when trying to add a marker without shadow in its icon.
\item Fixed a bug where popup content would not update on {\ttfamily set\+Content} call. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/94}{\texttt{\#94}}
\item Fixed a bug where double click zoom wouldn\textquotesingle{}t work if popup is opened on map click
\item Fixed a bug with click propagation on popup close button. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/99}{\texttt{\#99}}
\item Fixed inability to remove Image\+Overlay layer.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Browser bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug where paths would not appear in IE8.
\item Fixed a bug where there were occasional slowdowns before zoom animation in Web\+Kit. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/123}{\texttt{\#123}}
\item Fixed incorrect zoom animation \& popup styling in Opera 11.\+11.
\item Fixed popup fade animation in Firefox and Opera.
\item Fixed a bug where map isn\textquotesingle{}t displayed in Firefox when there\textquotesingle{}s an {\ttfamily img \{ max-\/width:\+ 100\% \}} rule.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\#\#\# Mobile browsers bugfixes


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a bug that prevented panning on some Android 2.\+1 (and possibly older) devices. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/84}{\texttt{\#84}}
\item Disabled zoom animation on Android by default because it\textquotesingle{}s buggy on some devices (will be enabled back when it\textquotesingle{}s stable enough). \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/32}{\texttt{\#32}}
\item Fixed a bug where map would occasionally break while multi-\/touch-\/zooming on i\+OS. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/32}{\texttt{\#32}}
\item Fixed a bug that prevented panning/\+clicking on Android 3 tablets. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/121}{\texttt{\#121}}
\item Fixed a bug that prevented panning/\+clicking on Opera Mobile. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/138}{\texttt{\#138}}
\item Fixed potentional memory leak on Web\+Kit when removing tiles, thanks to \href{https://github.com/Scalar4eg}{\texttt{@Scalar4eg}}. \href{https://github.com/Leaflet/Leaflet/issues/107}{\texttt{\#107}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\#\# 0.\+1 (2011-\/05-\/13)

Initial Leaflet release.
